rule("CORE: (TIMER) SET START TIME")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Global;
	}

	conditions
	{
		(Is Game In Progress && !Is Waiting For Players) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Global.BERSERK[0] = 0;
		Global.MAX_TIME = 121;
		Set Match Time(121);
		Global.BossIgnitedDamageTaken = 0;
		Pause Match Time;
		Global.X[0] = 0;
		Global.checkpoint = 0;
		Create HUD Text(All Players(All Teams), Custom String("{0} / 10", Global.X[0]), Custom String("BOSS"), Custom String(
			"SOULS COLLECTED"), Right, -100, Color(Team 1), Color(Team 1), Color(Yellow), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(All Teams), Null, Null, Custom String("-------------"), Right, -2, Color(White), Color(White), Color(
			White), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(All Teams), Null, Null, Custom String("-------------"), Right, -1, Color(White), Color(White), Color(
			White), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Global.BERSERK[1] = -1;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (BOSS) ALL - RESISTANCE STAT")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player.current_hero != Hero Of(Event Player);
	}

	actions
	{
		Event Player.current_hero = Hero Of(Event Player);
		If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Ashe));
			Global.BossResistanceStat = 0.360;
		Else If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Jetpack Cat));
			Global.BossResistanceStat = 0.220;
		Else If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Mauga));
			Global.BossResistanceStat = 0.420;
		Else If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Symmetra));
			Global.BossResistanceStat = 0.470;
		Else If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Zarya));
			Global.BossResistanceStat = 0.260;
		Else If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Soldier: 76));
			Global.BossResistanceStat = 0.250;
		Else If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Mei));
			Global.BossResistanceStat = 0.180;
		Else If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Junkrat));
			Global.BossResistanceStat = 0.370;
		Else If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Echo) || Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Mercy));
			Global.BossResistanceStat = 0.330;
		Else If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Vendetta) || Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Illari));
			Global.BossResistanceStat = 0.350;
		Else If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Venture) || Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Winston));
			Global.BossResistanceStat = 0.550;
		Else If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Reaper) || Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Sojourn) || Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(
				Wrecking Ball));
			Global.BossResistanceStat = 0.480;
		Else If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Reinhardt) || Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Ramattra) || Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(
				Domina));
			Global.BossResistanceStat = 0.200;
		Else If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Brigitte) || Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Lifeweaver) || Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(
				Pharah) || Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Sigma));
			Global.BossResistanceStat = 0.200;
		Else If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(D.Va) || Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Junker Queen) || Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Moira)
				|| Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Orisa) || Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Widowmaker));
			Global.BossResistanceStat = 0.500;
		Else;
			Global.BossResistanceStat = 0.400;
		End;
		End;
		Wait(0.100, Ignore Condition);
		Loop If Condition Is True;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TIMER) TEAM DEATH")
{
	event
	{
		Player Died;
		Team 2;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Is Waiting For Players == False;
	}

	actions
	{
		Global.X[0] += 1;
		Set Team Score(Team 1, Global.X[0]);
		Set Match Time(Match Time + 15);
		Small Message(All Players(All Teams), Custom String("{0} Down: +15 seconds", Hero Icon String(Hero Of(Event Player))));
		Skip If(Event Player != Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), 4);
		Big Message(All Players(All Teams), Custom String("{0} DEAD {0}", Hero Icon String(Hero(Mercy))));
		Set Match Time(Match Time + 30);
		Small Message(All Players(Team 1), Custom String("SOUL KEEPER BONUS: +15 SECONDS"));
		Small Message(All Players(Team 2), Custom String("SOUL KEEPER PENALTY: +15 SECONDS"));
		Skip If(Is Hero Being Played(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), 3);
		Set Match Time(Match Time + 20);
		Small Message(All Players(All Teams), Custom String("NO SOUL KEEPER: +5 SECONDS"));
		Global.DeadTeam[Slot Of(Event Player)] = True;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TIMER) MAX TIME")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Global;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Global.BERSERK[2] != 1;
		Is Game In Progress == True;
		Is Waiting For Players == False;
		Match Time > Global.MAX_TIME;
	}

	actions
	{
		Small Message(All Players(Team 1), Custom String("MAX TOTAL TIME"));
		Set Match Time(Global.MAX_TIME);
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TIMER) TIME CHECKPOINT")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Global;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Is Game In Progress == True;
		Match Time <= 1;
		Is Waiting For Players == False;
	}

	actions
	{
		Set Match Time(Global.MAX_TIME);
		Big Message(All Players(Team 1), Custom String("Checkpoint Lost"));
		Big Message(All Players(Team 2), Custom String("Checkpoint Reached"));
		Global.checkpoint += 1;
		Global.X[0] = Global.checkpoint * -1;
		Set Team Score(Team 1, Global.X[0]);
	}
}

rule("CORE: (SCORE) SET SCORE + DISABLE BUILT IN SCORE")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Global;
	}

	actions
	{
		Set Team Score(Team 1, Global.X[0]);
		Disable Built-In Game Mode Scoring;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (SCORE) TEAM RES")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Mercy;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Is Game In Progress == True;
		Is Waiting For Players == False;
		Is Using Ability 2(Event Player) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Wait(1.707, Ignore Condition);
		Skip If(!Is Using Ability 2(Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2)) || Is Alive(Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2))
			== False, 10);
		Global.X[0] -= 1;
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Skip If(Global.BERSERK[0] > 0, 1);
		Skip If(Match Time <= 31, 4);
		Skip If(Match Time >= 16, 2);
		Set Match Time(1);
		Skip(1);
		Set Match Time(Match Time - 14.900);
		Small Message(All Players(All Teams), Custom String("RESURRECTION: -15 SECONDS"));
		Set Team Score(Team 1, Global.X[0]);
	}
}

rule("CORE: (SCORE) BOSS DEATH")
{
	event
	{
		Player Died;
		Team 1;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Is Dead(All Players(Team 1)) == True;
		Is Waiting For Players == False;
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 1);
		Set Status(All Players(Team 2), Null, Invincible, 10);
		Disable Built-In Game Mode Announcer;
		Wait(1.800, Ignore Condition);
		Modify Team Score(Team 2, 10);
		Enable Built-In Game Mode Announcer;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (MSGS) FINAL BOSS HIT MSG")
{
	event
	{
		Player Dealt Final Blow;
		Team 2;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Is Dead(All Players(Team 1)) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 2);
		Big Message(All Players(All Teams), Custom String("{0} {1} Eliminated Boss {0}", Hero Icon String(Hero Of(Event Player)),
			Event Player));
		Set Slow Motion(33);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players == False, 1);
		Small Message(All Players(All Teams), Custom String("{0} {1} Eliminated Boss {0}", Hero Icon String(Hero Of(Event Player)),
			Event Player));
	}
}

		Destroy HUD Text(Global.X[2]);
		Wait(0.030, Ignore Condition);
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.X[3]);
		Wait(0.030, Ignore Condition);
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.X[4]);
		Wait(0.030, Ignore Condition);
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.X[5]);
		Wait(0.030, Ignore Condition);
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.X[6]);
		Wait(0.030, Ignore Condition);

			White), Color(White), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
	}

			White), Color(White), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);

rule("CORE: (TEAM) MERCY: RES HEALING UP (H) + RES HEALING VAR (H)")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Mercy;
	}

	conditions
	{
		(Is Using Ability 2(Event Player) || !Global.H[0]) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		If(Global.H[0] != False);
			Global.H[0] = False;
		Else;
			Global.H[0] = True;
			Wait Until(Is Using Ability 2(Event Player) != True, 99999);
			Wait(1, Ignore Condition);
			Global.H[0] = False;
		End;
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Loop If Condition Is True;
	}
}

rule("CORE: DOUBLE JUMP .................. PRE-MADE")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		All;
		All;

		Event Player.PlayerFX_1 -= 1;
	}

{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Mercy;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Is Using Ability 2(Event Player) == False;
		Event Player.S == True;
		Is Waiting For Players == False;
	}

	actions
	{
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.M);
		Global.Res_CD = 5;
		Event Player.S = False;
		Set Healing Received(Event Player, 20);
		Skip If(Is Alive(Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2)) == False, 3);
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.Mercy_State);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(All Teams), Custom String("{0} {1}", Round To Integer(Global.Res_CD, Up), Hero Icon String(Hero(
			Mercy))), Null, Null, Top, -5, Color(White), Color(White), Color(Yellow), Visible To and String, Visible Always);
		Global.Mercy_State = Last Text ID;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) MERCY: RES COOLDOWN")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Global;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Is Waiting For Players == False;
		Global.Res_CD > 0;
	}

	actions
	{
		Wait(1, Ignore Condition);
		Global.Res_CD -= 1;
		Wait(1, Ignore Condition);
		Global.Res_CD -= 1;
		Wait(1, Ignore Condition);
		Global.Res_CD -= 1;
		Wait(1, Ignore Condition);
		Global.Res_CD -= 1;
		Wait(1, Ignore Condition);
		Global.Res_CD -= 1;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) MERCY: HERO ICON ON + HERO ICON OFF")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Mercy);
	}

	actions
	{
		Create Icon(All Players(Team 2), Event Player, Halo, Visible To and Position, Color(Yellow), True);
		Event Player.I = Last Created Entity;
		Wait Until(Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Mercy), 99999);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Destroy Icon(Event Player.I);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Loop If Condition Is True;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) ALL - GENERAL SWITCH")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		All;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player.current_hero != Hero Of(Event Player);
	}

	actions
	{
		Event Player.current_hero = Hero Of(Event Player);
		If(Team Of(Event Player) == Team 2);
			Stop Holding Button(Event Player, Button(Crouch));
			Set Damage Dealt(Event Player, 100);
			Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_1);
			Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_2);
			Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_3);
			If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Bastion));
				Set Max Health(Event Player, 99.379);
			Else If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Mercy) || Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Domina));
				Set Max Health(Event Player, 98.765);
			Else If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Moira) || Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Freja) || Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Sojourn)
					);
				Set Max Health(Event Player, 99.206);
			Else If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Tracer));
				Set Max Health(Event Player, 99.861);
				Event Player.base_shields = Max Health Of Type(Event Player, Shields);
			Else If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Mei));
				Set Max Health(Event Player, 99.638);
			Else If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Doomfist));
				Set Max Health(Event Player, 99.099);
			Else If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Reinhardt));
				Set Max Health(Event Player, 99.502);
			Else If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Ramattra));
				Set Max Health(Event Player, 99.550);
			Else If(Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Winston) && Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Bastion) && Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Mei)
					&& Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Echo));
				Set Max Health(Event Player, 100);
			End;
		End;
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Illari) || Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Jetpack Cat));
			Set Knockback Dealt(Event Player, 0);
		Else If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Zenyatta));
			Set Knockback Dealt(Event Player, 4);
		Else;
			Set Knockback Dealt(Event Player, 100);
		End;
		Event Player.base_health = Max Health(Event Player);
		Event Player.base_shields = Max Health Of Type(Event Player, Shields);
		Wait(0.100, Ignore Condition);
		Loop If Condition Is True;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (BOSS) Mercy - Valkyrie Health")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		Mercy;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Is Using Ultimate(Event Player) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Set Damage Dealt(Event Player, 149);
		Set Healing Received(Event Player, 200);
		Set Move Speed(Event Player, 50);
		Set Max Health(Event Player, 166.458);
		Wait(0.001, Ignore Condition);
		disabled Heal(Event Player, Null, Health(Event Player) * 0.666);
		Set Player Health(Event Player, Health(Event Player) * 1.666);
		Heal(Event Player, Event Player, 1);
		Event Player.M = True;
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 3);
		Play Effect(All Players(Team 2), Good Explosion, Color(White), Event Player, 10);
		Create Effect(All Players(Team 2), Sparkles, Color(White), Event Player, 5, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.U = Last Created Entity;
	}
}

	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;

		Set Healing Received(Event Player, 100);
		Set Move Speed(Event Player, 100);

		disabled Set Player Health(Event Player, Health(Event Player) * 0.600);
		Wait(0.001, Ignore Condition);
		Set Max Health(Event Player, 99.875);
		Event Player.M = False;
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 2);
		Play Effect(All Players(Team 2), Bad Explosion, Color(White), Event Player, 3);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.U);
	}

rule("CORE: (BOSS) Mercy - FAST HEAL ABILITY")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		Mercy;
	}

	conditions
	{

	}

	{
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = False;
		Global.BOSS_AbilityCD = 30;

		Play Effect(All Players(Team 1), Ring Explosion Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 100);
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_AbilityKey);

			Left, 1, Color(Orange), Color(White), Color(Yellow), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityKey = Last Text ID;
		Event Player.Z[0] = True;
		Wait(2.400, Ignore Condition);
		Event Player.Z[0] = False;
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_AbilityKey);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(Team 1), Round To Integer(Global.BOSS_AbilityCD, Up), Custom String("Half Life"), Custom String(
			"Healing"), Left, 1, Color(Orange), Color(White), Color(Yellow), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityKey = Last Text ID;
		Chase Global Variable At Rate(BOSS_AbilityCD, 0, 1, None);
		Wait(30, Ignore Condition);
		Stop Chasing Global Variable(BOSS_AbilityCD);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityCD = 0;
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = True;
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_AbilityKey);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(Team 1), Input Binding String(Button(Ability 1)), Custom String("Half Life"), Custom String("Healing"),
			Left, 1, Color(White), Color(White), Color(Yellow), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);

rule("CORE: (BOSS) REIN - FLAME ON")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		Reinhardt;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player.F == 0;
		Has Spawned(Event Player) == True;
		disabled Is Waiting For Players == False;
		Has Status(Event Player, Hacked) == False;
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Event Player.primary_charge == 2, 1);
		Event Player.primary_charge += 1;
		Skip If(Event Player.primary_charge == 0, 5);
		Set Ability 2 Enabled(Event Player, True);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 3);
		Clear Status(Event Player, Burning);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Bad Pickup Effect, Color(Red), Event Player, 1);
		Set Status(Event Player, Null, Burning, 9999);
		Skip If(Event Player.primary_charge != 2, 1);
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, F);
		Event Player.F = 5;
		Skip If(Event Player.primary_charge != 2, 3);
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_AbilityKey);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(Team 1), Custom String("{0} {0}", Icon String(Fire)), Custom String("CHARGES OF"), Custom String(
			"FIRE STRIKE"), Left, 1, Color(Red), Color(White), Color(Red), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityKey = Last Text ID;
		Skip If(Event Player.primary_charge != 1, 3);
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_AbilityKey);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(Team 1), Custom String("{0} {1}", Icon String(Fire), Round To Integer(Event Player.F, Up)),
			Custom String("CHARGES OF"), Custom String("FIRE STRIKE"), Left, 1, Color(Red), Color(White), Color(Red),
			Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityKey = Last Text ID;
		Skip If(Event Player.primary_charge != 0, 3);
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_AbilityKey);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(Team 1), Custom String("{0} {1}", Icon String(No), Round To Integer(Event Player.F, Up)),
			Custom String("CHARGES OF"), Custom String("FIRE STRIKE"), Left, 1, Color(Red), Color(White), Color(Red),
			Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityKey = Last Text ID;
	}
}

		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_AbilityKey);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(Team 1), Custom String("{0} {1}", Icon String(Fire), Round To Integer(Event Player.F, Up)),
			Custom String("CHARGES OF"), Custom String("FIRE STRIKE"), Left, 1, Color(Red), Color(White), Color(Red),
			Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityKey = Last Text ID;
		Skip If(Event Player.primary_charge != 0, 3);
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_AbilityKey);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(Team 1), Custom String("{0} {1}", Icon String(No), Round To Integer(Event Player.F, Up)),

	}

	actions
	{
		disabled Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 3);
		Skip If(Event Player.S == Null, 2);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.S);
		Event Player.S = Null;
		Skip If(Event Player.D && Event Player == Players On Hero(Hero(Genji), Team 1), 1);
		Event Player.D = 0;
		disabled Skip If(Event Player == Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 1) || Event Player == Players On Hero(Hero(Symmetra), Team 1)
			|| Event Player == Players On Hero(Hero(Zenyatta), Team 1) || Event Player == Players On Hero(Hero(Torbjörn), Team 1), 1);
		disabled Set Ability 1 Enabled(Event Player, True);
	}
}

rule("CORE: (BOSS) GENJI - DASH LOCK/UNLOCK")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		Genji;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Genji);
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Event Player.D == 1, 1);
		Set Ability 1 Enabled(Event Player, False);
		Skip If(Event Player.D == 5, 1);
		Set Ability 1 Enabled(Event Player, True);
		Wait(0.001, Ignore Condition);
		Loop If Condition Is True;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (BOSS) TRACER - ULTIMATE USE")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		Tracer;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Global.W == True;
		Global.BOSS_AbilityCD == 100;
		Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Ultimate)) == True;
		Event Player.Stunned != True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Global.BOSS_AbilityCD = 4;
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Good Explosion, Color(Sky Blue), Event Player, 2);
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_AbilityKey);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(Team 1), Round To Integer(Global.BOSS_AbilityCD, Up), Custom String("WARP SPEED"), Custom String(
			"ENGAGED"), Left, 1, Color(White), Color(Aqua), Color(Aqua), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityKey = Last Text ID;
		Wait(0.050, Ignore Condition);
		Skip If(Event Player.PlayerFX_3 == Null, 1);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_3);
		Create Effect(All Players(Team 1), Ring, Color(Orange), Event Player, 0.500, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.PlayerFX_3 = Last Created Entity;
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 4);
		Skip If(Event Player.PlayerFX_1 == Null, 1);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_1);
		Create Effect(All Players(Team 1), Good Aura, Color(Orange), Event Player + Vector(0, Event Player.Z[4], 0) + Facing Direction Of(
			Event Player), 1.360, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.PlayerFX_1 = Last Created Entity;
		Set Damage Dealt(Event Player, 200);
		Set Move Speed(Event Player, 250);
		Wait(0.250, Ignore Condition);
		Set Invisible(Event Player, All);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring Explosion Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 150);
		Chase Global Variable At Rate(BOSS_AbilityCD, 0, 1, None);
		Wait(3.750, Ignore Condition);
		Stop Chasing Global Variable(BOSS_AbilityCD);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityCD = 0;
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_AbilityKey);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(Team 1), Custom String("{0}%", Round To Integer(Global.BOSS_AbilityCD, Down)), Custom String(
			"Charging Ultimate Ability"), Custom String("WARP SPEED: x2 DMG + INVISIBLE"), Left, 1, Color(Orange), Color(Orange), Color(
			White), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityKey = Last Text ID;
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Explosion Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 100);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Bad Explosion, Color(Orange), Event Player, 2);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_1);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_3);
		Set Invisible(Event Player, None);
		Set Move Speed(Event Player, 100);
		Set Damage Dealt(Event Player, 100);
		Global.W = False;
		Set Ultimate Charge(Event Player, Global.BOSS_AbilityCD);
	}
}

rule("CORE: (BOSS) BRIG - BASH OFF")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		Brigitte;
	}

	conditions
	{
		(Is Firing Secondary(Event Player) && Is Firing Primary(Event Player)) == True;
		Is Waiting For Players == False;
	}

rule("CORE: (BOSS) MOIRA - HEAL USING")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		Moira;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Global.W == True;
		Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Primary Fire)) == True;
		Global.BOSS_AbilityCD > 0;
		Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Secondary Fire)) == False;
		Is Using Ability 1(Event Player) == False;
		Is Using Ability 2(Event Player) == False;
		Is Using Ultimate(Event Player) == False;
		Event Player.Stunned != True;
		Normalized Health(Event Player) != 1;
	}

	actions
	{
		Global.B = True;
		Wait(0.050, Abort When False);
		Heal(Event Player, Event Player, 10.050);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityCD -= 1;
		Loop If Condition Is True;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (BOSS) MOIRA - HEAL RECHARGE")

	}

rule("CORE: (BOSS) MOIRA - HEAL CANCEL")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		Moira;
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(!Is Using Ability 1(Event Player) && !Is Using Ability 2(Event Player) && !Is Using Ultimate(Event Player)
			&& !Has Status(Event Player, Hacked) && !Has Status(Event Player, Knocked Down) && !Has Status(
			Event Player, Asleep) && !Has Status(Event Player, Frozen) && !Has Status(Event Player, Stunned)
			 && True, 1);
		Global.W = False;
		Skip If(!Is Using Ability 1(Event Player) && !Is Using Ability 2(Event Player) && !Is Using Ultimate(Event Player)
			 && !Has Status(Event Player, Hacked) && !Has Status(Event Player, Knocked Down) && !Has Status(
			Event Player, Asleep) && !Has Status(Event Player, Frozen) && !Has Status(Event Player, Stunned)
			 && Global.BOSS_AbilityCD == 100, 1);
		Skip(1);
		Global.W = True;
		Wait(0.001, Ignore Condition);
		Loop If Condition Is True;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (BOSS) SYM - SHIELD ABILITY")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		Symmetra;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle == True;
		Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Ability 1)) == True;
		Event Player.Stunned != True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = False;
		Global.BOSS_AbilityCD = 6;
		Chase Global Variable At Rate(BOSS_AbilityCD, 0, 1, None);
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_AbilityKey);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(Team 1), Round To Integer(Global.BOSS_AbilityCD, Up), Custom String("PHOTOGEL"), Custom String(
			"ABSORPTION SHIELD"), Left, 1, Color(Aqua), Color(White), Color(Aqua), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityKey = Last Text ID;
		Skip If(Event Player.PlayerFX_2 == Null, 1);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_2);
		Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Energy Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 100, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.PlayerFX_2 = Last Created Entity;
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 4);
		Skip If(Event Player.PlayerFX_1 == Null, 1);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_1);
		Create Effect(All Players(Team 1), Good Aura, Color(Aqua), Event Player + Vector(0, Event Player.Z[4], 0) + Facing Direction Of(
			Event Player), 1.360, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.PlayerFX_1 = Last Created Entity;
		Skip If(Event Player.PlayerFX_3 == Null, 1);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_3);
		Create Effect(All Players(Team 1), Ring, Color(Aqua), Event Player, 0.500, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.PlayerFX_3 = Last Created Entity;
		Skip If(Event Player.PlayerFX_0 == Null, 1);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_0);
		Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Orb, Color(Team 1), Event Player, 2, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.PlayerFX_0 = Last Created Entity;
		Global.BossDamageReceived *= 0.100;
		Set Damage Received(Event Player, Global.BossDamageReceived);
		Wait(6, Ignore Condition);
		Stop Chasing Global Variable(BOSS_AbilityCD);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityCD = 21;
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_AbilityKey);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(Team 1), Round To Integer(Global.BOSS_AbilityCD, Up), Custom String("PHOTOGEL"), Custom String(
			"ABSORPTION SHIELD"), Left, 1, Color(Orange), Color(White), Color(Aqua), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityKey = Last Text ID;
		Chase Global Variable At Rate(BOSS_AbilityCD, 0, 1, None);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring Explosion, Color(Team 1), Event Player, 3);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_0);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_2);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_3);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_1);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring Explosion Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 100);
		Global.BossDamageReceived *= 10;
		Set Damage Received(Event Player, Global.BossDamageReceived);
		Wait(21, Ignore Condition);
		Stop Chasing Global Variable(BOSS_AbilityCD);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityCD = 0;
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = True;
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_AbilityKey);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(Team 1), Input Binding String(Button(Ability 1)), Custom String("PHOTOGEL"), Custom String(
			"ABSORPTION SHIELD"), Left, 1, Color(White), Color(White), Color(Aqua), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityKey = Last Text ID;
		Play Effect(All Players(Team 1), Buff Impact Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 30);
	}
}

		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Null, Null, String("{0} {1}", Custom String("\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n"), String(
			"{0} {1}", Custom String("damage: "), Icon String(Arrow: Down))), Top, 8, Color(White), Color(White), Color(Black),
			Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.charge_hud = Last Text ID;
		Wait(0.100, Ignore Condition);
		Global.W = False;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (BOSS) CASS - DODGE ABILITY")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		Cassidy;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle == True;
		(Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Ability 1)) && Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Crouch))) == True;
		Velocity Of(Event Player) != 0;
		Event Player.U == 0;
		Is Using Ultimate(Event Player) == False;
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Event Player.Stunned, 20);
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = False;
		Global.BOSS_AbilityCD = 12;
		Chase Global Variable At Rate(BOSS_AbilityCD, 0, 1, None);
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_AbilityKey);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(Team 1), Round To Integer(Global.BOSS_AbilityCD, Up), Custom String("EXTENDED"), Custom String(
			"COMBAT ROLL"), Left, 1, Color(Orange), Color(White), Color(Orange), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityKey = Last Text ID;
		Apply Impulse(Event Player, Vector(X Component Of(Velocity Of(Event Player)), Y Component Of(Velocity Of(Event Player)),
			Z Component Of(Velocity Of(Event Player))), 40, To World, Incorporate Contrary Motion);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Explosion Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 50);
		Wait(12, Ignore Condition);
		Stop Chasing Global Variable(BOSS_AbilityCD);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityCD = 0;
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = True;
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_AbilityKey);
		Skip If(Event Player.U != 0, 2);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(Team 1), Custom String("{0}+{1}", Input Binding String(Button(Ability 1))), Custom String("EXTENDED"),
			Custom String("COMBAT ROLL"), Left, 1, Color(White), Color(White), Color(Orange), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityKey = Last Text ID;
		Skip If(Event Player.U == 0, 2);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(Team 1), Icon String(No), Custom String("EXTENDED"), Custom String("COMBAT ROLL"), Left, 1, Color(Red),
			Color(White), Color(Orange), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityKey = Last Text ID;
		Play Effect(All Players(Team 1), Buff Impact Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 25);
	}
}

		Wait(0.250, Ignore Condition);

		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, F);
		Event Player.F = 15;
		Global.BossFrozen = -1;

		Small Message(All Players(Team 1), Custom String("Whole Hog Frozen: 15 seconds"));
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_AbilityKey);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(Team 1), Custom String("{0} {1}", Ability Icon String(Hero(Mei), Button(Ultimate)), Round To Integer(
			Event Player.F, Up)), Custom String("THAWING"), Custom String("WHOLE HOG"), Left, 1, Color(Sky Blue), Color(White), Color(
			Sky Blue), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);

		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_3);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 2);

		Event Player.PlayerFX_3 = Last Created Entity;
	}

rule("CORE: (BOSS) HOG - FIRE DMG SET")
{
	event
	{
		Player Took Damage;
		Team 2;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Is Hero Being Played(Hero(Roadhog), Team 1) == True;
		Is Using Ultimate(Players On Hero(Hero(Roadhog), Team 1)) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Event Player.Z[2] = True;
		Set Status(Event Player, All Players(Team 1), Burning, 3);
		Event Player.Z[1] = 3;
		Wait(1, Ignore Condition);
		Abort If(!Event Player.Z[2]);
		Event Player.Z[1] -= 1;
		Wait(1, Ignore Condition);
		Abort If(!Event Player.Z[2]);
		Event Player.Z[1] -= 1;
		Wait(1, Ignore Condition);
		Abort If(!Event Player.Z[2]);
		Event Player.Z[1] -= 1;
		Skip If(Event Player.Z[1] != 0, 2);
		Event Player.Z[2] = False;
		Clear Status(Event Player, Burning);
	}
}

rule("CORE: (AFX) PLAYER SOUL UP")
{
	event
	{
		Player Died;
		Team 2;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Is Waiting For Players == False;
		Is Hero Being Played(Hero(Mercy), Team 2) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Event Player == Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), 17);
		Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Cloud, Color(Yellow), Event Player, 0.010, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.U = Last Created Entity;
		Create Icon(All Players(All Teams), Event Player + Up * 1, Skull, Visible To and Position, Color(Red), True);
		Event Player.Y[0] = Last Created Entity;
		Create In-World Text(All Players(Team 1), Hero Icon String(Hero Of(Event Player)), Event Player + Up * 0.250, 1.500, Do Not Clip,
			Visible To Position and String, Color(White), Default Visibility);
		Event Player.Y[1] = Last Text ID;
		Event Player.Y[3] = 8;
		Create In-World Text(All Players(Team 1), Event Player.Y[3], Event Player + Up * 1.500, 1.666, Do Not Clip,
			Visible To Position and String, Color(White), Default Visibility);
		Event Player.Y[2] = Last Text ID;
		Create In-World Text(Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), Custom String("REVIVE!"), Event Player + Up * 3, 2, Do Not Clip,
			Visible To Position and String, Color(Yellow), Default Visibility);
		Event Player.Y[5] = Last Text ID;
		Create In-World Text(Remove From Array(All Players(Team 2), Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2)), Custom String("DEFEND"),
			Event Player + Up * 3, 2, Do Not Clip, Visible To Position and String, Color(Orange), Default Visibility);
		Event Player.Y[6] = Last Text ID;
		Create In-World Text(All Players(Team 1), Custom String("GUARD"), Event Player + Up * 3, 2, Do Not Clip,
			Visible To Position and String, Color(Orange), Default Visibility);
		Event Player.Y[7] = Last Text ID;
		Wait(7.080, Ignore Condition);
		Event Player.Y[3] = 1;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (AFX) PLAYER SOUL TIMER")
{
	event
	{
		Player Died;
		Team 2;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Is Waiting For Players == False;
		Is Alive(Event Player) == False;
		disabled Event Player.Y[3] >= 0;
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Event Player == Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), 3);
		Wait(1, Ignore Condition);
		Event Player.Y[3] -= 1;
		Loop If Condition Is True;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (AFX) PLAYER SOUL DOWN")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;

		Destroy In-World Text(Event Player.Y[5]);
		Destroy In-World Text(Event Player.Y[6]);
		Destroy In-World Text(Event Player.Y[7]);
		Global.DeadTeam[Slot Of(Event Player)] = False;
	}
}

rule("Res Msg: Set 1 ................. SQUIDWARD")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Mercy;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player.E > 0;
		disabled Is Waiting For Players == False;
	}

	actions
	{
		Event Player.A = Sorted Array(Event Player.C, 1 - Dot Product(Facing Direction Of(Event Player), Direction Towards(Eye Position(
			Event Player), Position Of(Current Array Element) + Vector(0, Distance Between(Position Of(Current Array Element),
			Eye Position(Current Array Element)) * 0.500, 0))));
		Create HUD Text(All Players(Team 1), Custom String("Resurrecting {0}", Hero Icon String(Hero Of(Event Player.A))), Null, Null,
			Right, 0, Color(Red), Color(White), Color(White), String, Default Visibility);
		Global.ResMsg1_Feed = Last Text ID;
		Skip If(!Is Waiting For Players, 1);
		Small Message(All Players(All Teams), Custom String("Resurrecting {0}", Hero Icon String(Hero Of(Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy),
			Team 2).A))));
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 1);
		Big Message(All Players(All Teams), Custom String("Resurrecting {0}", Hero Icon String(Hero Of(Event Player.A))));
		Create HUD Text(All Players(Team 2), Custom String("Resurrecting {0}", Hero Icon String(Hero Of(Event Player.A))), Null, Null,
			Right, 0, Color(Sky Blue), Color(White), Color(White), String, Default Visibility);
		Global.ResMsg2_Feed = Last Text ID;
		Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring, Color(Yellow), Event Player.A, 2.500, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.PlayerFX_3 = Last Created Entity;
		Event Player.E = 0;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (MAP) OASIS CITY CENTER - BOUND LOOP")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		All;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Current Map == Map(Oasis City Center);
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Distance Between(Event Player, Vector(144, 4, 248.270)) > 42, 1);
		Skip(2);
		Play Effect(Event Player, Debuff Impact Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 50);
		Apply Impulse(Event Player, Vector Towards(Event Player, Vector(144, 4, 248.270)), Max(5.500, Speed Of(Event Player)), To World,
			Cancel Contrary Motion);
		Skip If(Distance Between(Event Player, Vector(144, 4, 248.270)) > 44, 1);
		Skip(3);
		Play Effect(Event Player, Debuff Impact Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 50);
		Teleport(Event Player, Direction Towards(Event Player, Vector(144, 4, 248.270)) * (Distance Between(Event Player, Vector(144, 4,
			248.270)) - 42) + Position Of(Event Player));
		Set Status(Event Player, Null, Stunned, 0.100);
		Skip If(Distance Between(Event Player, Vector(119.500, 0, 186.500)) <= 36, 1);
		Skip(2);
		Play Effect(Event Player, Debuff Impact Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 50);
		Apply Impulse(Event Player, Vector Towards(Vector(119.500, 0, 186.500), Position Of(Event Player)), Max(7, Speed Of(Event Player)),
			To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
		Skip If(Distance Between(Event Player, Vector(82.500, 0, 223.500)) <= 36, 1);
		Skip(2);
		Play Effect(Event Player, Debuff Impact Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 50);
		Apply Impulse(Event Player, Vector Towards(Vector(82.500, 0, 223.500), Position Of(Event Player)), Max(7, Speed Of(Event Player)),
			To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
		Skip If(Distance Between(Event Player, Vector(82.500, 0, 223.500)) < 34, 1);
		Skip(3);
		Play Effect(Event Player, Debuff Impact Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 50);
		Teleport(Event Player, Vector(118.700, 1, 232.800));
		Set Status(Event Player, Null, Stunned, 0.100);
		Skip If(Distance Between(Event Player, Vector(119.500, 0, 186.500)) < 34, 1);
		Skip(3);
		Play Effect(Event Player, Debuff Impact Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 50);
		Teleport(Event Player, Vector(128.200, 1, 223));
		Set Status(Event Player, Null, Stunned, 0.100);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Loop If Condition Is True;
	}
}

rule("ROLES: DEF-single lock condition")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Is Hero Being Played(Hero(Mercy), Team 2) == True;
		Count Of(Filtered Array(All Players(Team 2), Current Array Element.Z[3] == 1)) == 1;
		Is Waiting For Players == False;
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Event Player == Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), 2);
		Skip If(Array Contains(Global.A[1], Hero Of(Event Player)), 1);
		Set Player Allowed Heroes(Event Player, Remove From Array(Allowed Heroes(Event Player), Global.A[1]));
		Skip If(Event Player.Z[3] != 1, 1);
		Set Player Allowed Heroes(Event Player, Remove From Array(Allowed Heroes(Event Player), Global.A[2]));
	}
}

rule("ROLES: DEF-double lock condition")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Count Of(Filtered Array(All Players(Team 2), Current Array Element.Z[3] == 1)) == 2;
		Is Waiting For Players == False;
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Event Player.Z[3] == 1, 2);
		Set Player Allowed Heroes(Event Player, Remove From Array(Allowed Heroes(Event Player), Hero(Mercy)));
		Set Player Allowed Heroes(Event Player, Remove From Array(Allowed Heroes(Event Player), Global.A[1]));
		Skip If(Event Player.Z[3] != 1, 2);
		Set Player Allowed Heroes(Event Player, Append To Array(Allowed Heroes(Event Player), Global.A[2]));
		Set Player Allowed Heroes(Event Player, Append To Array(Allowed Heroes(Event Player), Hero(Mercy)));
	}
}

rule("ROLES: DEF+mercy unlock condition")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		(!Is Hero Being Played(Hero(Mercy), Team 2) && Count Of(Filtered Array(All Players(Team 2),
			Current Array Element.Z[3] == 2)) < 2) == True;
		Count Of(Filtered Array(All Players(Team 2), Current Array Element.Z[3] == 1)) < 2;
		Is Waiting For Players == False;
	}

	actions
	{
		Set Player Allowed Heroes(Event Player, Append To Array(Allowed Heroes(Event Player), Hero(Mercy)));
		Set Player Allowed Heroes(Event Player, Append To Array(Allowed Heroes(Event Player), Global.A[1]));
	}
}

rule("ROLES: ENF-double lock condition")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Count Of(Filtered Array(All Players(Team 2), Current Array Element.Z[3] == 2)) == 2;
		Is Waiting For Players == False;
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Event Player.Z[3] == 2, 2);
		Set Player Allowed Heroes(Event Player, Remove From Array(Allowed Heroes(Event Player), Hero(Mercy)));
		Set Player Allowed Heroes(Event Player, Remove From Array(Allowed Heroes(Event Player), Global.A[2]));
		Skip If(Event Player.Z[3] != 2, 2);
		Set Player Allowed Heroes(Event Player, Append To Array(Allowed Heroes(Event Player), Global.A[1]));
		Set Player Allowed Heroes(Event Player, Append To Array(Allowed Heroes(Event Player), Hero(Mercy)));
	}
}

		Global.DeadTeam = False;

rule("ROLES: (TIMER) START MATCH TIME")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Global;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Is Assembling Heroes == False;
		Is Game In Progress == True;
		Is True For All(All Players(All Teams), Has Spawned(Current Array Element)) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Wait(0.001, Ignore Condition);
		Skip If(Is True For Any(All Players(All Teams), Has Spawned(Current Array Element) == False), 6);
		Skip If(Global.A[0], 1);
		Big Message(All Players(All Teams), Custom String("3... 2... 1..."));
		disabled Clear Status(All Players(All Teams), Phased Out);
		disabled Set Invisible(All Players(All Teams), None);
		Global.A[0] = True;
		Wait(4, Ignore Condition);
		Unpause Match Time;
	}
}

rule("MAPS: Chateau Guillard")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		All;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		(Current Map == Map(Château Guillard) || Current Map == Map(Château Guillard)) == True;
		Y Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)) < -0.050;
		(Has Spawned(Event Player) && !Is Waiting For Players) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Z Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)) >= 67.900 && Z Component Of(Position Of(Event Player))
			<= 85.500 && X Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)) >= 199 && X Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)) <= 213, 17);
		Teleport(Event Player, Nearest Walkable Position(Event Player));
		Start Throttle In Direction(Event Player, Vector(0, 0, 0), 0, To Player, Replace existing throttle, Direction and Magnitude);
		Wait(0.016, Restart When True);
		Set Status(Event Player, Null, Knocked Down, 9999);
		Wait(0.016, Restart When True);
		Set Status(Event Player, Null, Phased Out, 9999);
		Wait(0.016, Restart When True);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Debuff Impact Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 100);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Good Pickup Effect, Color(White), Event Player, 2);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.ringout_FX);
		Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring, Color(White), Event Player, 0.500, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.ringout_FX = Last Created Entity;
		Wait(2, Restart When True);
		Big Message(Event Player, Custom String("{0} OUT OF BOUNDS {0}", Icon String(No)));
		Clear Status(Event Player, Knocked Down);
		Clear Status(Event Player, Phased Out);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.ringout_FX);
		Stop Throttle In Direction(Event Player);
		Wait(0.024, Restart When True);
		Loop If Condition Is True;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (AFX) PLAYER SOUL UP (no mercy)")

	event
	{
		Player Died;
		Team 2;
		All;
	}

	{
		Is Waiting For Players == False;
		Is Hero Being Played(Hero(Mercy), Team 2) == False;
	}

	actions
	{

		Event Player.U = Last Created Entity;
		Create Icon(All Players(All Teams), Event Player + Up * 1, Skull, Visible To and Position, Color(Red), True);
		Event Player.Y[0] = Last Created Entity;
		Create In-World Text(All Players(Team 1), Hero Icon String(Hero Of(Event Player)), Event Player + Up * 0.250, 1.500, Do Not Clip,
			Visible To Position and String, Color(White), Default Visibility);
		Event Player.Y[1] = Last Text ID;
		Event Player.Y[3] = 7;
		Create In-World Text(All Players(Team 1), Event Player.Y[3], Event Player + Up * 1.500, 1.666, Do Not Clip,
			Visible To Position and String, Color(White), Default Visibility);
		Event Player.Y[2] = Last Text ID;
		Create In-World Text(All Players(All Teams), Custom String("NO MERCY!"), Event Player + Up * 3, 2, Do Not Clip,
			Visible To Position and String, Color(Red), Default Visibility);
		Event Player.Y[5] = Last Text ID;
		Wait(7.080, Ignore Condition);
		Event Player.Y[3] = 0;
	}
}

{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Global.X[0] < 0;
	}

	actions
	{

		Skip If(Absolute Value(Global.X[0]) >= 5, 1);
		Skip If(Health(Event Player) - Absolute Value(13 * Absolute Value(Global.X[0])) <= 0.100, 1);
		Damage(Event Player, Null, Absolute Value(13 * Absolute Value(Global.X[0])));
		Loop If Condition Is True;
		Abort If Condition Is False;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (BOSS) ORISA: FORTIFY RESISTANCE+AMMO")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		Orisa;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Is Using Ability 1(Event Player) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Global.BossDamageReceived *= 1.450;
		Set Damage Received(Event Player, Global.BossDamageReceived);
		Remove Health Pool From Player(Event Player.shield_pool);
		Add Health Pool To Player(Event Player, Health, 22.223, False, False);
		Event Player.shield_pool = Last Created Health Pool;
		Wait Until(!Is Using Ability 1(Event Player), 5.200);
		Global.BossDamageReceived *= 100 / 145;
		Set Damage Received(Event Player, Global.BossDamageReceived);
		Remove Health Pool From Player(Event Player.shield_pool);
	}
}

			Ability 2))), Custom String("STUN DAMAGE"), Left, 10, Color(Red), Color(White), Color(Red), Visible To and String,

		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = True;
		Event Player.Ability_Bool = False;
		Event Player.primary_charge = 5;
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, primary_charge);
	}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) ASHE - SPAWN")

	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;

		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, secondary_charge);
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, timer);

		Event Player.secondary_charge = Color(White);
		Event Player.timer = 10;

			Ashe), Button(Ability 1)), Event Player.primary_charge), Top, 8.100, Color(White), Color(White), Event Player.secondary_charge,
			Visible To String and Color, Default Visibility);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players == False, 1);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Null, Null, Custom String(
			" \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n {0} : {1} \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n", Ability Icon String(Hero(Ashe), Button(
			Ability 1)), Event Player.primary_charge), Top, 8, Color(White), Color(White), Event Player.secondary_charge,
			Visible To String and Color, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.charge_hud[0] = Last Text ID;
		disabled Create HUD Text(Event Player, Null, Null, Custom String(" \r\n			{0} {0} [ {1} ]", Custom String(
			"                                                                                              "),
			Event Player.primary_charge), Top, 9, Color(White), Color(White), Event Player.secondary_charge, Visible To String and Color,
			Default Visibility);
		Event Player.team_abilityHUD[4] = Last Text ID;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) ASHE - COACH GUN USE")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Ashe;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Is Using Ability 1(Event Player) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, timer);
		Skip If(Event Player.primary_charge != 2, 8);
		Wait(0.500, Ignore Condition);
		Event Player.primary_charge = 1;
		Event Player.secondary_charge = Custom Color(255 - Event Player.timer * 15.500, 165 - Event Player.timer * 6.500,
			0 + Event Player.timer * 10, 255 - Event Player.timer * 15.500);
		Event Player.timer = 10;
		Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, timer, 0, 1, Destination and Rate);
		Wait(0.040, Ignore Condition);
		Set Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 1), 0.096);
		Skip(7);
		Skip If(Event Player.primary_charge != 1, 6);
		Wait(0.540, Ignore Condition);
		Event Player.primary_charge = 0;
		Event Player.secondary_charge = Custom Color(255 - Event Player.timer * 15.500, 165 - Event Player.timer * 6.500,
			0 + Event Player.timer * 10, 255 - Event Player.timer * 15.500);
		Set Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 1), Event Player.timer);
		Event Player.timer = 10;
		Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, timer, 0, 1, Destination and Rate);
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) ASHE - COACH GUN RESET")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Ashe;
	}

	conditions
	{
		((Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 1)) < 0.116 && Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 1)) > 0.100) || (
			Event Player.timer <= 0 && Event Player.primary_charge < 2)) == True;
		Is Using Ability 1(Event Player) == False;
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Event Player.primary_charge != 1, 6);
		Set Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 1), 0.096);
		Event Player.primary_charge = 2;
		Event Player.secondary_charge = Color(White);
		Event Player.timer = 10;
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, timer);
		Skip(5);
		Skip If(Event Player.primary_charge != 0, 5);
		Event Player.primary_charge = 1;
		Event Player.secondary_charge = Custom Color(255 - Event Player.timer * 15.500, 165 - Event Player.timer * 6.500,
			0 + Event Player.timer * 10, 255 - Event Player.timer * 15.500);
		disabled Set Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 1), 0);
		disabled Event Player.timer = 10;
		disabled Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, timer, 0, 1, Destination and Rate);
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) ASHE - HUD CLOSE")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Ashe;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Distance Between(Event Player, All Players(Team 1)) < 25;
		Entity Exists(All Players(Team 1)) == True;
		Is In Line of Sight(Eye Position(Event Player), All Players(Team 1), Barriers Do Not Block LOS) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0]);
		Destroy Progress Bar HUD Text(Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0]);
		disabled Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Ability Icon String(Hero(Ashe), Button(Secondary Fire)), Custom String(
			"Bonus damage within 25m - in range"), Custom String("HARDSHELL SHOTS"), Left, 10, Color(Green), Color(White), Color(Green),
			Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0] = Last Text ID;
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud[1]);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Null, Null, Custom String("effective hardshell range"), Top, 8.500, Color(White), Color(White),
			Color(Green), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.charge_hud[1] = Last Text ID;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) VENTURE - USE STUN")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Venture;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player.Stunned != True;
		(Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Ultimate)) && Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Secondary Fire))
			 && Event Player.Ability_Toggle) == True;
		Event Player.primary_charge == 0;
		Is Firing Secondary(Event Player) == True;
		Is Using Ability 1(Event Player) == False;
	}

	actions
	{
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = False;
		Event Player.Ability_Bool = True;
		Set Ultimate Charge(Event Player, Ultimate Charge Percent(Event Player) - 8);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Buff Impact Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 100);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.X);
		Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Baptiste Immortality Field Protected Effect, Color(Yellow), Event Player, 100,
			Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.X = Last Created Entity;
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0]);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Icon String(Warning), Custom String("ACTIVE"), Custom String("DRILL DASH STUN"), Left, 10, Color(
			Aqua), Color(Orange), Color(White), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0] = Last Text ID;
	}
}

		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Custom String("{0} {1}", Ability Icon String(Hero(Junker Queen), Button(Secondary Fire)),
			Icon String(Dizzy)), Custom String("Damage with knife to stun Boss"), Custom String("Jagged Blade Stun"), Left, 10, Color(Red),
			Color(White), Color(Red), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0] = Last Text ID;
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, secondary_charge);
		Event Player.secondary_charge = 0;
		Event Player.primary_charge = Custom String("G.READY");
	}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) Ana - Heal Dart Warning")
{
	event
	{
		Player Dealt Healing;
		Team 2;
		Ana;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Hero Of(Healee) != Hero(Mercy);
		Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 2)) <= 10;
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle == 0;
		Is Using Ability 2(Event Player) == False;
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Healee == Event Player, 23);
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = 1;
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud[0]);
		Wait(0.033, Ignore Condition);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 6);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Null, Custom String(
			"\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\nHEAL DART WARNING:"),
			Null, Top, 8, Color(White), Color(White), Color(White), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.charge_hud[0] = Last Text ID;
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_1);
		Wait(0.033, Ignore Condition);
		Create Effect(Event Player, Good Aura, Color(Purple), Event Player + Vector(0, Event Player.Z[4], 0) + Facing Direction Of(
			Event Player), 1.750, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.PlayerFX_1 = Last Created Entity;
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players == False, 2);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Null, Custom String(
			"\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\nHEAL DART WARNING:"), Null, Top, 8, Color(
			White), Color(White), Color(White), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.charge_hud[0] = Last Text ID;
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud[1]);
		Wait(0.333, Ignore Condition);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Null, Custom String("NEGLIGIBLE HEALING + LOSE ULTIMATE"), Null, Top, 8.100, Color(Sky Blue), Color(
			White), Color(White), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.charge_hud[1] = Last Text ID;
		Wait(3.333, Ignore Condition);
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = 0;
		Wait(0.033, Ignore Condition);
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud[0]);
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud[1]);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_1);

rule("CORE: (TEAM) BRIG - ABILITY USE")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Brigitte;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle == True;
		Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Reload)) == True;
		Is Alive(Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2)) == True;
		Event Player.Stunned != True;
		Global.mercyArmourBool == False;
		Event Player.Aim[0] == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = False;
		Event Player.Aim[0] = False;
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud[0]);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.charge_hud[1]);
		Global.mercyArmourBool = True;
		Heal(Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), Event Player, 250);
		Add Health Pool To Player(Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), Armor, 50, True, True);
		Global.brig_armour = Last Created Health Pool;
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Good Pickup Effect, Color(Yellow), Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), 1);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Buff Impact Sound, Color(White), Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), 50);
		Play Effect(Event Player, Buff Impact Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 50);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 3);
		Destroy Effect(Global.mercyArmourFX);
		Skip If(Is Communicating Any Emote(Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2)), 3);
		Create Effect(Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), Good Aura, Color(White), Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2) + Vector(0,
			Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2).Z[4], 0) + Facing Direction Of(Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2)), 1.660,
			Visible To Position and Radius);
		Global.mercyArmourFX = Last Created Entity;
		Skip(4);
		Wait Until(!Is Communicating Any Emote(Event Player), 99999);
		Skip If(!Global.mercyArmourBool, 2);
		Create Effect(Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), Good Aura, Color(White), Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2) + Vector(0,
			Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2).Z[4], 0) + Facing Direction Of(Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2)), 1.660,
			Visible To Position and Radius);
		Global.mercyArmourFX = Last Created Entity;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) BRIG - ARMOUR BROKEN")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Brigitte;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Global.mercyArmourBool == True;
		Health(Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2)) <= 100;
	}

	actions
	{
		Wait(0.033, Abort When False);
		Global.mercyArmourBool = False;
		Skip If(Event Player.Ability_Toggle, 2);
		Event Player.mercyArmourCD = 24;
		Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, mercyArmourCD, 0, 1, Destination and Rate);
		Remove Health Pool From Player(Global.brig_armour);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Good Explosion, Color(Orange), Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), 0.500);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Buff Impact Sound, Color(White), Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), 50);
		Play Effect(Event Player, Buff Impact Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 50);
		Skip If(Is Alive(Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2)), 1);
		Global.mercyArmourDead = True;
		Destroy Effect(Global.mercyArmourFX);
		Skip If(Event Player.Ability_Toggle, 7);
		Wait(24, Ignore Condition);
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, mercyArmourCD);
		Event Player.mercyArmourCD = 0;
		Skip If(Is Hero Being Played(Hero(Mercy), Team 2) == True, 1);
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = False;
		Skip If(Is Hero Being Played(Hero(Mercy), Team 2) == False, 1);
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = True;
	}
}

		Event Player.mercyArmourCD = 0;
		Skip If(Is Hero Being Played(Hero(Mercy), Team 2) == True, 1);
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = False;
		Skip If(Is Hero Being Played(Hero(Mercy), Team 2) == False, 1);
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = True;
	}
}

			Custom String("MERCY ARMOUR"), Left, 10, Color(White), Color(White), Color(Yellow), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);

rule("CORE: (TEAM) MOIRA - PRIMARY WARNING")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Moira;
	}

	conditions
	{
		(Is Alive(Event Player) && Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Primary Fire)) && !Is Using Ability 2(Event Player)
			 && !Is Firing Primary(Event Player)) == True;
		Ability Resource(Event Player, Button(Primary Fire)) > 23;
		Event Player.primary_charge == 0;
	}

	actions
	{
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud[0]);
		Wait(0.033, Ignore Condition);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 1);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Null, Custom String(
			"\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\nPRIMARY HEAL WARNING:"),
			Null, Top, 8, Color(White), Color(White), Color(White), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players == False, 1);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Null, Custom String(
			"\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\nPRIMARY HEAL WARNING:"), Null, Top, 8, Color(
			White), Color(White), Color(White), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.charge_hud[0] = Last Text ID;
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud[1]);
		Wait(0.333, Ignore Condition);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Null, Custom String("BIOTIC HEAL ORB MUST BE ACTIVE"), Null, Top, 8.100, Color(Sky Blue), Color(
			White), Color(White), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.charge_hud[1] = Last Text ID;
		Wait(3.333, Ignore Condition);
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud[0]);
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud[1]);
	}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) BAP - ABILITY USE")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Baptiste;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Is Using Ability 1(Event Player) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = True;
		Event Player.primary_charge = Players Within Radius(Eye Position(Event Player), 12, Team 2, Surfaces And Enemy Barriers);
		Event Player.Ability_Bool = 5;
		Wait(0.150, Ignore Condition);
		Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, Ability_Bool, 0, 1, Destination and Rate);
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0]);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Custom String(" {0} ", Round To Integer(Event Player.Ability_Bool, Up)), Custom String(
			"{0} allies affected", Round To Integer(Count Of(Event Player.primary_charge), To Nearest)), Custom String(
			"over shields burst"), Left, 10, Color(Aqua), Color(Aqua), Color(Sky Blue), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0] = Last Text ID;
		Wait(5, Ignore Condition);
		Event Player.primary_charge = Null;
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, Ability_Bool);
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = False;
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0]);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Ability Icon String(Hero(Baptiste), Button(Ability 1)), Custom String("cooldown"), Custom String(
			"over shields burst"), Left, 10, Color(Orange), Color(White), Color(Sky Blue), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0] = Last Text ID;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) ALL - BAP OVER SHIELDS UP")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Is True For Any(Players On Hero(Hero(Baptiste), Team 2), Array Contains(Current Array Element.primary_charge, Event Player))
			== True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Remove Health Pool From Player(Event Player.overshields);
		Add Health Pool To Player(Event Player, Shields, Event Player.base_health * 0.200, True, False);
		Event Player.overshields = Last Created Health Pool;
		Event Player.base_shields = Max Health Of Type(Event Player, Shields);
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) ECHO - ULTIMATE USE")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Echo;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle == True;
		Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Ultimate)) == True;
		(!Event Player.Stunned && !Has Status(Event Player, Rooted)) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Set Ultimate Ability Enabled(Event Player, False);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring Explosion Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 100);
		Event Player.primary_charge = 12;
		Wait(0.016, Abort When False);
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0]);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Custom String("- {0} -", Round To Integer(Event Player.primary_charge, Up)), Custom String(
			"ability active"), Custom String("cooldown reduction"), Left, 10, Color(White), Color(Red), Color(Sky Blue),
			Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0] = Last Text ID;
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = False;
		Event Player.Ability_Bool = True;
		Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, primary_charge, 0, 1, Destination and Rate);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_1);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_2);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_3);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 2);
		Create Effect(Event Player, Good Aura, Color(Sky Blue), Event Player + Vector(0, Event Player.Z[4], 0) + Facing Direction Of(
			Event Player), 1.666, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.PlayerFX_1 = Last Created Entity;
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create Effect(All Players(Team 2), Echo Cloning Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 200, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.PlayerFX_2 = Last Created Entity;
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Echo Cloning Effect, Color(Team 2), Event Player, 0.500, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.PlayerFX_3 = Last Created Entity;
	}
}

		Is Hero Being Played(Hero(Roadhog), Team 1) == True;
		Event Player.Z[2] == True;
		Event Was Health Pack == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Event Player.Z[2] = False;
		Clear Status(Event Player, Burning);
		Event Player.Z[1] = 3;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (BOSS) JUNK - FIRE DMG FROZEN")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		Junkrat;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player == Players On Hero(Hero(Junkrat), Team 1);
		Has Status(Event Player, Frozen) == True;
		Is Waiting For Players == False;
	}

	actions
	{
		Event Player.X[0] = 0.100;
		Wait(0.250, Ignore Condition);
		Set Damage Dealt(Event Player, 100);
		Clear Status(Event Player, Burning);
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, F);
		Event Player.F = 15;
		Global.BossFrozen = -1;
		Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, F, 0, 1, Destination and Rate);
		Small Message(All Players(Team 1), Custom String("FIRE DAMAGE Frozen: 15 seconds"));
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_AbilityKey);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(Team 1), Custom String("{0} {1}", Ability Icon String(Hero(Mei), Button(Ultimate)), Round To Integer(
			Event Player.F, Up)), Custom String("THAWING"), Custom String("FIRE DAMAGE"), Left, 1, Color(Sky Blue), Color(White), Color(
			Sky Blue), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityKey = Last Text ID;
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_3);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 2);
		Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Cloud, Color(White), Event Player, 1, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.PlayerFX_3 = Last Created Entity;
		Wait(15, Restart When True);
		Abort If(Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Junkrat));
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_3);
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_AbilityKey);
		Skip If(Is Portrait On Fire(Event Player) == False, 5);
		Set Damage Dealt(Event Player, 133.200);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Bad Pickup Effect, Color(Red), Event Player, 1);
		Set Status(Event Player, Null, Burning, 9999);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(Team 1), Icon String(Fire), Custom String("you're on fire!"), Custom String("fire damage"), Left, 1,
			Color(Orange), Color(White), Color(Orange), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityKey = Last Text ID;
		Skip If(Is Portrait On Fire(Event Player) == True, 2);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(Team 1), Icon String(Warning), Custom String("get kills to deal more damage"), Custom String(
			"fire damage"), Left, 1, Color(Red), Color(White), Color(Orange), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityKey = Last Text ID;
		Event Player.X[0] = 0;
		Global.BossFrozen = 0;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (BOSS) ASHE - DYNAMITE FROZEN")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		Ashe;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player == Players On Hero(Hero(Ashe), Team 1);
		Has Status(Event Player, Frozen) == True;
		disabled Is Waiting For Players == False;
	}

	actions
	{
		Disallow Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 2));
		Skip If(Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 2)) == 0, 1);
		Event Player.X[0] = Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 2));
		Event Player.X[0] = Event Player.X[0];
		Wait(0.250, Ignore Condition);
		Set Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 2), 0);
		Set Ability 2 Enabled(Event Player, False);
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, F);
		Event Player.F = 15;
		Global.BossFrozen = -1;
		Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, F, 0, 1, Destination and Rate);
		Small Message(All Players(Team 1), Custom String("Dynamite Frozen: 15 seconds"));
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_AbilityKey);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(Team 1), Custom String("{0} {1}", Ability Icon String(Hero(Mei), Button(Ultimate)), Round To Integer(
			Event Player.F, Up)), Custom String("THAWING"), Custom String("DYNAMITE"), Left, 1, Color(Sky Blue), Color(White), Color(
			Sky Blue), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityKey = Last Text ID;
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_3);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 2);
		Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Cloud, Color(White), Event Player, 1, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.PlayerFX_3 = Last Created Entity;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (BOSS) ALL - ABILITY 2 SET")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Has Spawned(Event Player) == True;
		Is Alive(Event Player) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Mercy) || Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Zarya) || Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Lifeweaver),
			2);
		Set Ability 2 Enabled(Event Player, True);
		Allow Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 2));
		Skip If(Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Mercy) && Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Zarya) && Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Lifeweaver),
			2);
		Set Ability 2 Enabled(Event Player, False);
		Disallow Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 2));
	}
}

		Set Ability 1 Enabled(Event Player, True);
		Allow Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 1));
		Skip If(Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Mercy) && Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Zenyatta) && Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Sombra)
			&& Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Symmetra) && Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Ramattra), 2);
		Set Ability 1 Enabled(Event Player, False);

rule("CORE: (BOSS) WIDOW: SHIELD POOL")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		Widowmaker;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Has Spawned(Event Player) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Set Max Health(Event Player, 99.971);
		Remove Health Pool From Player(Global.BOSS_HealthPools[0]);
		Remove Health Pool From Player(Global.BOSS_HealthPools[1]);
		Add Health Pool To Player(Event Player, Shields, 25, True, False);
		Global.BOSS_HealthPools[0] = Last Created Health Pool;
		Set Player Health(Event Player, 900);
		Event Player.base_health = Max Health(Event Player);
		Event Player.base_shields = Max Health Of Type(Event Player, Shields);
	}
}

rule("CORE: (BOSS) REIN - FIRE THAW")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		Reinhardt;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Global.BossFrozen == -1;
		(Event Player.F == 0 || Is Dead(Event Player)) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_3);
		Skip If(Event Player.primary_charge < 1, 4);
		Set Ability 2 Enabled(Event Player, True);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 1);
		Set Status(Event Player, Null, Burning, 9999);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Bad Pickup Effect, Color(Red), Event Player, 1);
		Event Player.F = 5;
		Skip If(Event Player.primary_charge < 2, 1);
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, F);
		Skip If(Is Alive(Event Player), 3);
		Set Ability 2 Enabled(Event Player, True);
		Event Player.primary_charge += 1;
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_AbilityKey);
		Global.BossFrozen = 0;
		Wait(0.050, Ignore Condition);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_3);
	}
}

		Event Player.N = Last Created Entity;

rule("CORE: (TEAM) PHARAH - MERCY BEACON PLACEMENT")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Pharah;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Ability 2)) == True;
		(!Event Player.Stunned && !Has Status(Event Player, Rooted)) == True;
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle == True;
		Event Player.Ability_Bool == False;
		Is Alive(Event Player) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = False;
		Global.MercyBeacon[0] = Eye Position(Event Player);
		Global.MercyBeacon[1] = Altitude Of(Event Player);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Buff Explosion Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 50);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Orb, Color(Team 2), Global.MercyBeacon[0], 1, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Global.MercyBeacon[2] = Last Created Entity;
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Good Aura, Color(Team 2), Global.MercyBeacon[0], 1.100, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Global.MercyBeacon[3] = Last Created Entity;
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Beacon Sound, Color(Aqua), Global.MercyBeacon[0], 100, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Global.MercyBeacon[4] = Last Created Entity;
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring, Color(Team 2), Global.MercyBeacon[0] - Vector(0, Global.MercyBeacon[1], 0), 6,
			Visible To Position and Radius);
		Global.MercyBeacon[5] = Last Created Entity;
		Event Player.primary_charge = 10;
		Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, primary_charge, 0, 1, Destination and Rate);
		Event Player.Ability_Bool = True;
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create Icon(Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), Global.MercyBeacon[0], Eye, Visible To and Position, Color(Aqua), True);
		Global.MercyBeacon[6] = Last Created Entity;
		Create Effect(Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), Beacon Sound, Color(White), Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), 100,
			Visible To Position and Radius);
		Global.MercyBeacon[8] = Last Created Entity;
		Set Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 2), -1);
		Set Ability 2 Enabled(Event Player, False);
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) MERCY - PHARAH MERCY BEACON USE")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Mercy;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Is True For Any(Players On Hero(Hero(Pharah), Team 2), Current Array Element.Ability_Bool == True) == True;
		Is Alive(Event Player) == True;
		Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Interact)) == True;
		Absolute Value(X Component Of(Global.MercyBeacon[0]) - X Component Of(Position Of(Event Player))) <= 5;
		Absolute Value(Z Component Of(Global.MercyBeacon[0]) - Z Component Of(Position Of(Event Player))) <= 5;
	}

	actions
	{
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.MercyBeacon[7]);
		Filtered Array(Players On Hero(Hero(Pharah), Team 2), Current Array Element.Ability_Bool).Ability_Toggle = False;
		Filtered Array(Players On Hero(Hero(Pharah), Team 2), Current Array Element.Ability_Bool).primary_charge = 30;
		Set Ability Cooldown(Filtered Array(Players On Hero(Hero(Pharah), Team 2), Current Array Element.Ability_Bool), Button(
			Ability 2), 30);
		Players On Hero(Hero(Pharah), Team 2).Ability_Bool = False;
		Set Ability 2 Enabled(Filtered Array(Players On Hero(Hero(Pharah), Team 2), !Current Array Element.Ability_Bool), True);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring Explosion Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 50);
		Wait(0.050, Ignore Condition);
		Skip If(!Is Using Ability 2(Event Player), 7);
		Set Status(Event Player, Filtered Array(Players On Hero(Hero(Pharah), Team 2), Current Array Element.primary_charge >= 29),
			Unkillable, 0.700);
		Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring, Color(Team 2), Event Player, 0.500, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Global.MercyBeacon[9] = Last Created Entity;
		Wait(0.700, Ignore Condition);
		Clear Status(Event Player, Unkillable);
		Destroy Effect(Global.MercyBeacon[9]);
		Skip If(Is Using Ability 2(Event Player), 5);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Good Explosion, Color(White), Event Player, 1);
		Wait(0.050, Ignore Condition);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Good Pickup Effect, Color(Team 2), Event Player, 1);
		Wait(0.050, Ignore Condition);
		Teleport(Event Player, Position Of(Global.MercyBeacon[0]));
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Destroy Effect(Global.MercyBeacon[2]);
		Destroy Effect(Global.MercyBeacon[3]);
		Destroy Effect(Global.MercyBeacon[4]);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Destroy Effect(Global.MercyBeacon[5]);
		Destroy Icon(Global.MercyBeacon[6]);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.MercyBeacon[7]);
		Destroy Effect(Global.MercyBeacon[8]);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Buff Explosion Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 20);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Good Explosion, Color(White), Event Player, 1);
	}
}

		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Brigitte Repair Pack Armor Effect, Color(White), Event Player, 1);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Brigitte Repair Pack Impact Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 1);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Brigitte Repair Pack Armor Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 1);
	}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) RAM - HOT LOOP")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Ramattra;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Is Alive(Event Player) == True;
		(Has Status(Event Player, Stunned) != True && Has Status(Event Player, Knocked Down) != True && Has Status(Event Player, Frozen)
			!= True && Has Status(Event Player, Asleep) != True && Has Status(Event Player, Hacked) != True && True) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Heal(Filtered Array(Players Within Radius(Eye Position(Event Player), Event Player.primary_charge, Team 2,
			Surfaces And Enemy Barriers), Is Alive(Current Array Element) && Current Array Element != Event Player), Event Player,
			Event Player.PassiveAOEHeal);
		Heal(Event Player, Event Player, 0.750 * Event Player.PassiveAOEHeal);
		Wait(0.100, Abort When False);
		Skip If(Event Player.secondary_charge != 10, 3);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Heal Target Active Effect, Color(White), Event Player, 1);
		Event Player.secondary_charge = 1;
		Skip(6);
		Skip If(Event Player.secondary_charge != 5 || Event Player.PassiveAOEHeal < 2, 2);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Heal Target Active Effect, Color(White), Event Player, 1);
		Skip(2);
		Skip If((Event Player.secondary_charge != 2 && Event Player.secondary_charge != 7) || (Event Player.PassiveAOEHeal < 4), 1);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Heal Target Active Effect, Color(White), Event Player, 1);
		Event Player.secondary_charge += 1;
		Loop If Condition Is True;
	}
}

	{
		Player Died;
		Team 2;
		All;

		Skip If(Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Zenyatta), 1);

		Skip If(Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Winston), 1);
		Set Ultimate Charge(Event Player, Ultimate Charge Percent(Event Player) - 50);
		Skip If(Ultimate Charge Percent(Event Player) >= 0, 1);
		Set Ultimate Charge(Event Player, 0);
	}
}

			Current Array Element != Event Player))), Left, 10, Color(Purple), Color(Yellow), Color(Black), Visible To and String,
			Default Visibility);
		Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0] = Last Text ID;
	}

			Custom String("WHIRLWIND STUN: HOLD {0}", Input Binding String(Button(Ability 1))), Left, 9.500, Custom Color(255, 215, 175,
			255), Color(White), Color(White), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.team_abilityHUD[4] = Last Text ID;
		Play Effect(Event Player, Buff Explosion Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 50);
		Skip If(Event Player.secondary_charge == 0, 2);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Round To Integer(Event Player.secondary_charge, Up), Custom String("COOLDOWN"), Custom String(
			"WHIRLWIND STUN", Input Binding String(Button(Ability 1))), Left, 9.500, Color(Orange), Color(Orange), Color(White),
			Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.team_abilityHUD[4] = Last Text ID;
	}
}
