rule("CORE: (TEAM) VENDETTA: WHIRLWIND STUN USE")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Vendetta;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player.secondary_charge == 0;
		(Ultimate Charge Percent(Event Player) >= 25 && Ultimate Charge Percent(Event Player) < 100) == True;
		Is Using Ability 1(Event Player) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Wait(0.400, Abort When False);
		Skip If(!Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Ability 1)) || Ultimate Charge Percent(Event Player)
			< 25 || Ultimate Charge Percent(Event Player) >= 100 || !Is Using Ability 1(Event Player), 14);
		Set Status(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 4, Team 1, Surfaces), Event Player, Stunned, 0.650);
		Set Ultimate Charge(Event Player, Ultimate Charge Percent(Event Player) - 25);
		Event Player.secondary_charge = 15;
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.team_abilityHUD[4]);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Round To Integer(Event Player.secondary_charge, Up), Custom String("COOLDOWN"), Custom String(
			"WHIRLWIND STUN", Input Binding String(Button(Ability 1))), Left, 9.500, Color(Orange), Color(Orange), Color(White),
			Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.team_abilityHUD[4] = Last Text ID;
		Skip If(Count Of(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 4, Team 1, Surfaces)) < 1, 6);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Debuff Impact Sound, Color(White), Players Within Radius(Event Player, 4, Team 1, Surfaces),
			800);
		Destroy Effect(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 4, Team 1, Surfaces).statusFX);
		Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Cassidy Flashbang Stunned Effect, Color(White), Players Within Radius(Event Player, 4,
			Team 1, Surfaces), 1, Visible To Position and Radius);
		All Players(Team 1).statusFX = Last Created Entity;
		Wait(0.650, Ignore Condition);
		Destroy Effect(All Players(Team 1).statusFX);
	}
}

rule("CORE: (ALL) START MATCH")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		All;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Is Waiting For Players == False;
		Global.A[0] == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Teleport(Event Player, Event Player.SpawnStats[0]);
		Set Status(Event Player, Null, Rooted, 4);
		Wait(4, Ignore Condition);
		Set Ultimate Charge(Event Player, Event Player.SpawnStats[1]);
		Clear Status(Event Player, Phased Out);
		Clear Status(Event Player, Unkillable);
		Set Invisible(Event Player, None);
		Big Message(Event Player, Custom String("READY! FIGHT!"));
		Skip If(Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Lúcio) || Team Of(Event Player) != Team 2, 1);
		Event Player.primary_charge = 0;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) REAP - ENERGY USE")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Reaper;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player.Stunned != True;
		(Event Player.Ability_Toggle && Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Secondary Fire)) && !Has Status(Event Player,
			Rooted) && !Is Using Ability 2(Event Player) && !Is Using Ultimate(Event Player)) == True;
		Event Player.secondary_charge != 1;
	}

	actions
	{
		Destroy In-World Text(Event Player.PlayerFX_1);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring Explosion Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 100);
		Event Player.primary_charge = 6;
		Wait(0.016, Abort When False);
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0]);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Custom String("- {0} -", Round To Integer(Event Player.primary_charge, Up)), Custom String(
			"ability active"), Custom String("the reaper energy  {0}", Icon String(Bolt)), Left, 10, Color(Blue), Color(Blue), Color(
			Black), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0] = Last Text ID;
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = False;
		Event Player.Ability_Bool = True;
		Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, primary_charge, 0, 1, Destination and Rate);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_1);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_2);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_3);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 2);
		Create Effect(Event Player, Good Aura, Color(Violet), Event Player + Vector(0, Event Player.Z[4], 0) + Facing Direction Of(
			Event Player), 1.666, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.PlayerFX_1 = Last Created Entity;
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create Effect(Remove From Array(All Players(All Teams), Event Player), Bad Aura, Color(Team 2), Event Player, 1,
			Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.PlayerFX_2 = Last Created Entity;
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring, Color(Team 2), Event Player, 0.500, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.PlayerFX_3 = Last Created Entity;
	}
}

		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;

	}

		Create Effect(All Players(Opposite Team Of(Team Of(Event Player))), Ring, Color(Rose), Position Of(Event Player) + Vector(0, 0.100,
			0), 1, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.Sombra[0] = Last Created Entity;
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.Sombra[1]);
		Create Effect(All Players(Opposite Team Of(Team Of(Event Player))), Bad Aura, Color(Rose), Position Of(Event Player) + Vector(0, 1,
			0), 1, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.Sombra[1] = Last Created Entity;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) RAM: HEALTH")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Ramattra;
	}

	actions
	{
		Remove Health Pool From Player(Event Player.health_pool);
		Remove Health Pool From Player(Event Player.shield_pool);
		Remove Health Pool From Player(Event Player.armour_pool);
		Add Health Pool To Player(Event Player, Armor, 163.392, True, False);
		Event Player.armour_pool = Last Created Health Pool;
		Add Health Pool To Player(Event Player, Health, 11.728, True, False);
		Event Player.health_pool = Last Created Health Pool;
		Event Player.base_health = Max Health(Event Player);
		Event Player.base_shields = Max Health Of Type(Event Player, Shields);
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, D);
		Event Player.D = 0;
	}
}

	}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) CASS - USE MEDS")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Cassidy;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player.Stunned != True;
		(Event Player.Ability_Toggle && Is Crouching(Event Player) && Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Ultimate))
			) == True;
		Is In Air(Event Player) == False;
	}

	actions
	{
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = False;
		Event Player.Ability_Bool = True;
		Start Holding Button(Event Player, Button(Crouch));
		Event Player.primary_charge = 3.300;
		Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, primary_charge, 0, 1, Destination and Rate);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Heal Target Active Effect, Color(Yellow), Event Player, 100);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Set Ultimate Charge(Event Player, Ultimate Charge Percent(Event Player) - 5);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Buff Impact Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 100);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.X);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Heal Target Effect, Color(Yellow), Event Player, 100, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.X = Last Created Entity;
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 1);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Null, Null, Custom String(
			"   \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n                              {0}", Round To Integer(
			Event Player.primary_charge, Up)), Top, 8, Color(White), Color(White), Color(Yellow), Visible To and String,
			Default Visibility);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players == False, 1);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Null, Null, Custom String(
			"   \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n                              {0}", Round To Integer(
			Event Player.primary_charge, Up)), Top, 8, Color(White), Color(White), Color(Yellow), Visible To and String,
			Default Visibility);
		Event Player.charge_hud = Last Text ID;
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0]);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Icon String(Plus), Custom String("PATCHING UP... {0}", Round To Integer(Event Player.primary_charge,
			Up)), Custom String("PATCH UP:  {0} + HOLD [crouch]", Input Binding String(Button(Ultimate))), Left, 10, Color(Yellow), Color(
			Yellow), Color(White), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0] = Last Text ID;
	}
}

		Event Player.Ability_Bool = False;

		Destroy Effect(Event Player.X);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);

			"PATCH UP"), Left, 10, Color(Orange), Color(Orange), Color(White), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0] = Last Text ID;
	}

	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Wrecking Ball;
	}

	conditions

			 && Event Player.Ability_Toggle) == True;
		Event Player.primary_charge == 0;

		Destroy Effect(Event Player.X);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Baptiste Immortality Field Protected Effect, Color(Yellow), Event Player, 100,
			Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.X = Last Created Entity;

		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Icon String(Warning), Custom String("ACTIVE"), Custom String("PILEDRIVE SLAM"), Left, 10, Color(
			Aqua), Color(Orange), Color(White), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);

	}
}

rule("MAPS: ANTI-ENVIRO actions")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		All;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		(Has Spawned(Event Player) && Current Map != Map(Ecopoint: Antarctica) && Current Map != Map(Hollywood)
			&& Current Map != Map(King's Row) && Current Map != Map(King's Row) && Current Map != Map(Temple of Anubis)
			&& Current Map != Map(Château Guillard) && Current Map != Map(Château Guillard) && Current Map != Map(Horizon Lunar Colony)
			&& Current Map != Map(Workshop Chamber) && Current Map != Map(Workshop Expanse) && Current Map != Map(Workshop Expanse)
			&& Current Map != Map(Workshop Island) && Current Map != Map(Workshop Island) && Current Map != Map(Workshop Green Screen))
			== True;
		(Y Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)) < Global.Enviro_Threshold && !Is Waiting For Players) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Current Map != Map(Kanezaka), 2);
		Teleport(Event Player, Vector(-18.800, 8.800, 40.200));
		Skip(4);
		Skip If(Current Map != Map(Hanamura) && Current Map != Map(Eichenwalde), 2);
		Call Subroutine(anti_enviro_OOM);
		Skip(1);
		Teleport(Event Player, Nearest Walkable Position(Event Player));
		Start Throttle In Direction(Event Player, Vector(0, 0, 0), 0, To Player, Replace existing throttle, Direction and Magnitude);
		Wait(0.001, Restart When True);
		Set Status(Event Player, Null, Knocked Down, 9999);
		Skip If(Team Of(Event Player) == Team 2, 2);
		Wait(0.001, Restart When True);
		Set Status(Event Player, Null, Phased Out, 9999);
		Wait(0.001, Restart When True);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Debuff Impact Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 100);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Good Pickup Effect, Color(White), Event Player, 2);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.ringout_FX);
		Skip If(Team Of(Event Player) == Team 2, 2);
		Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring, Color(White), Event Player, 0.500, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.ringout_FX = Last Created Entity;
		Skip If(Has Status(Event Player, Knocked Down), 8);
		Wait(2, Restart When True);
		Big Message(Event Player, Custom String("{0} OUT OF BOUNDS {0}", Icon String(No)));
		Stop Throttle In Direction(Event Player);
		Clear Status(Event Player, Phased Out);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.ringout_FX);
		Wait Until(!Is Using Ability 1(Event Player), 4.040);
		Set Status(Event Player, Null, Knocked Down, 4.444);
		Skip(5);
		Wait(2, Restart When True);
		Big Message(Event Player, Custom String("{0} OUT OF BOUNDS {0}", Icon String(No)));
		Clear Status(Event Player, Knocked Down);
		Stop Throttle In Direction(Event Player);
		Wait(0.900, Restart When True);
		Clear Status(Event Player, Phased Out);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.ringout_FX);
		Loop If Condition Is True;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) SIG - LEVITATION ON")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Sigma;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player.Stunned != True;
		(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Sigma) && !Has Status(Event Player, Rooted) && !Is Using Ultimate(Event Player)
			 && Event Player.Ability_Toggle) == True;
		Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Jump)) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Wait(0.250, Abort When False);
		Event Player.Ability_Bool = True;
		Set Gravity(Event Player, 20);
		Set Move Speed(Event Player, 40);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Moira Fade Disappear Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 50);
		Start Accelerating(Event Player, Up, 12.500, 1.500, To World, Direction Rate and Max Speed);
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0]);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create Progress Bar HUD Text(Event Player, Event Player.primary_charge, Custom String("LEVITATION"), Left, 10, Custom Color(0, 0,
			155, 245), Custom Color(30, 144, 255, 250), Visible To Values and Color, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0] = Last Text ID;
		Chase Player Variable Over Time(Event Player, primary_charge, 0, 4, Destination and Duration);
		Wait Until(!Event Player.Ability_Bool, 4);
		Stop Accelerating(Event Player);
		Skip If(!Event Player.Ability_Bool, 2);
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, primary_charge);
		Event Player.primary_charge = 0;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) SIG - LEVITATION OFF")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Sigma;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player.Ability_Bool == True;
		(!Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Jump)) || Is Dead(Event Player) || Has Status(Event Player, Hacked) || Has Status(
			Event Player, Asleep) || Has Status(Event Player, Knocked Down) || Has Status(Event Player, Frozen) || Has Status(Event Player,
			Rooted) || Has Status(Event Player, Stunned) || Is Using Ultimate(Event Player) || Is On Ground(Event Player)) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = False;
		Set Gravity(Event Player, 100);
		Set Move Speed(Event Player, 100);
		Event Player.Ability_Bool = False;
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Moira Fade Reappear Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 50);
		Wait(0.050, Ignore Condition);
		Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, primary_charge, 100, 25, Destination and Rate);
		Wait Until(Event Player.primary_charge == 100, 4.200);
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, primary_charge);
		Destroy Progress Bar HUD Text(Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0]);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Icon String(Arrow: Up), Custom String("HOLD  [{0}]  BUTTON", Input Binding String(Button(Jump))),
			Custom String("LEVITATION"), Left, 10, Color(Blue), Color(White), Color(Sky Blue), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0] = Last Text ID;
		Event Player.primary_charge = 100;
		Play Effect(Event Player, Buff Impact Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 25);
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = True;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (BOSS) ECHO - P.C. UP")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		Echo;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Ultimate Charge Percent(Event Player) < 100;
		Event Player.Stunned != True;
		(Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Ultimate)) && Event Player.Ability_Toggle && Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(
			Echo) && !Has Status(Event Player, Rooted) && !Is Duplicating(Event Player)) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = False;
		Event Player.Ability_Bool = True;
		Event Player.L = Position Of(Event Player);
		Event Player.N = Facing Direction Of(Event Player);
		Event Player.C = Y Component Of(Eye Position(Event Player));
		Event Player.F = Eye Position(Event Player) + Facing Direction Of(Event Player) * 500;
		Skip If(Speed Of In Direction(Event Player, Facing Direction Of(Event Player)) > 3.600, 1);
		Event Player.F += Facing Direction Of(Event Player) * Vector(9999, 0, 9999);
		Event Player.Aim = Vertical Facing Angle Of(Event Player);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Skip If(Event Player.Aim > 0, 4);
		Event Player.secondary_charge = -2 / 9 * Vertical Facing Angle Of(Event Player) + 0.600;
		Wait(0.025, Ignore Condition);
		Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, secondary_charge, 0, 33, None);
		Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, C, 1000, Event Player.secondary_charge, Destination and Rate);
		Skip If(Event Player.Aim <= 0, 1);
		Event Player.secondary_charge = 0;
		Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, L, Event Player.F, -1 / 9 * Event Player.Aim + 15, Destination and Rate);
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_AbilityKey);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Icon String(Bolt), Null, Custom String("CHARGE BOMB"), Left, 1, Custom Color(3, 5, 100, 255), Color(
			White), Color(Yellow), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityKey = Last Text ID;
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Baptiste Biotic Launcher Explosion Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 100);
		Play Effect(All Players(Team 1), Good Explosion, Color(Aqua), Event Player, 1);
		Play Effect(All Players(Team 2), Good Explosion, Color(Red), Event Player, 1);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_1);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create Effect(All Players(Team 1), Orb, Color(Aqua), Vector(X Component Of(Event Player.L), Event Player.C, Z Component Of(
			Event Player.L)), 1, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.PlayerFX_1 = Last Created Entity;
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_2);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create Effect(All Players(Team 2), Orb, Color(Orange), Vector(X Component Of(Event Player.L), Event Player.C, Z Component Of(
			Event Player.L)), 1, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.PlayerFX_2 = Last Created Entity;
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud);
	}
}

rule("CORE: (BOSS) ECHO - P.C. DOWN")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		Echo;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player.Ability_Bool == True;
		Event Player.secondary_charge == 0;
		Has Spawned(Event Player) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Event Player.Aim <= 0, 1);
		Event Player.secondary_charge = Event Player.Aim * 0.270;
		Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, secondary_charge, 25, 8, None);
		Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, C, -400, Event Player.secondary_charge, Destination and Rate);
	}
}

rule("CORE: (BOSS) ECHO - P.C. HIT Y")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		Echo;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player.Ability_Bool == True;
		Distance Between(Vector(X Component Of(Event Player.L), Event Player.C, Z Component Of(Event Player.L)), Ray Cast Hit Position(
			Vector(X Component Of(Event Player.L), Event Player.C, Z Component Of(Event Player.L)), Vector(0, -500, 0), All Players(
			Team 2), Event Player, True)) < 0.500;
	}

	actions
	{
		Event Player.primary_charge = 20;
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, secondary_charge);
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, C);
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, L);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Sombra EMP Explosion Effect, Color(Team 1), Vector(X Component Of(Event Player.L),
			Event Player.C, Z Component Of(Event Player.L)), 7);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring Explosion Sound, Color(White), Vector(X Component Of(Event Player.L), Event Player.C,
			Z Component Of(Event Player.L)), 100);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_1);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_2);
		Event Player.Ability_Bool = False;
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Damage(Remove From Array(Players Within Radius(Vector(X Component Of(Event Player.L), Event Player.C, Z Component Of(
			Event Player.L)), 3, Team 2, Surfaces), Event Player), Event Player, 6);
		Damage(Remove From Array(Players Within Radius(Vector(X Component Of(Event Player.L), Event Player.C, Z Component Of(
			Event Player.L)), 6, Team 2, Surfaces), Event Player), Event Player, 6);
		Damage(Remove From Array(Players Within Radius(Vector(X Component Of(Event Player.L), Event Player.C, Z Component Of(
			Event Player.L)), 9, Team 2, Surfaces), Event Player), Event Player, 6);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Damage(Remove From Array(Players Within Radius(Vector(X Component Of(Event Player.L), Event Player.C, Z Component Of(
			Event Player.L)), 12, Team 2, Surfaces), Event Player), Event Player, 6);
		Damage(Remove From Array(Players Within Radius(Vector(X Component Of(Event Player.L), Event Player.C, Z Component Of(
			Event Player.L)), 15, Team 2, Surfaces), Event Player), Event Player, 6);
		Set Ultimate Charge(Event Player, Ultimate Charge Percent(Event Player) + 1 * Count Of(Players Within Radius(Vector(X Component Of(
			Event Player.L), Event Player.C, Z Component Of(Event Player.L)), 15, Team 2, Surfaces)));
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_AbilityKey);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Round To Integer(Event Player.primary_charge, Up), Custom String("cooldown"), Custom String(
			"CHARGE BOMB"), Left, 1, Color(Orange), Color(Orange), Color(Sky Blue), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityKey = Last Text ID;
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 1);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Null, Null, Custom String(
			"   \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n                              {0}", Round To Integer(
			Event Player.primary_charge, Up)), Top, 8, Color(White), Color(White), Color(Aqua), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players == False, 1);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Null, Null, Custom String(
			"   \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n                              {0}", Round To Integer(
			Event Player.primary_charge, Up)), Top, 8, Color(White), Color(White), Color(Aqua), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.charge_hud = Last Text ID;
		Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, primary_charge, 0, 1, Destination and Rate);
		Wait(20, Ignore Condition);
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, primary_charge);
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_AbilityKey);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Custom String("- {0} -", Input Binding String(Button(Ultimate))), Custom String(
			"throw an energy bomb that\r\n			ignores shields and charges duplicate"), Custom String("CHARGE BOMB"), Left, 1, Color(White),
			Color(White), Color(Sky Blue), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityKey = Last Text ID;
		Event Player.secondary_charge = 1;
		Play Effect(Event Player, Buff Impact Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 25);
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 1);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Null, Null, Custom String(
			"   \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n                              {0}", Icon String(Bolt)), Top, 8,
			Color(White), Color(White), Color(Aqua), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players == False, 1);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Null, Null, Custom String(

		Damage(Remove From Array(Players Within Radius(Vector(X Component Of(Event Player.L), Event Player.C, Z Component Of(
			Event Player.L)), 9, Team 2, Surfaces), Event Player), Event Player, 6);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Damage(Remove From Array(Players Within Radius(Vector(X Component Of(Event Player.L), Event Player.C, Z Component Of(
			Event Player.L)), 12, Team 2, Surfaces), Event Player), Event Player, 6);
		Damage(Remove From Array(Players Within Radius(Vector(X Component Of(Event Player.L), Event Player.C, Z Component Of(
			Event Player.L)), 15, Team 2, Surfaces), Event Player), Event Player, 6);

rule("CORE: (TEAM) LW - HEAL CHARGE+")
{
	event
	{
		Player Dealt Damage;
		Team 2;
		Lifeweaver;
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Event Ability == Button(Melee), 4);
		Skip If(Event Player.primary_charge >= 100, 3);
		Skip If(!Event Was Critical Hit, 1);
		Event Player.primary_charge += 1.833;
		Event Player.primary_charge += 1.833;
		Skip If(Event Player.primary_charge <= 100, 1);
		Event Player.primary_charge = 100;
	}
}

			Custom Color(150, 140, 0, 220), Color(White), Visible To Values and Color, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0] = Last Text ID;

		Skip If(Hero Of(Event Player) == Hero(Lifeweaver), 1);
		Abort;
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0]);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Destroy Progress Bar HUD Text(Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0]);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Ability Icon String(Hero(Lifeweaver), Button(Primary Fire)), Custom String(
			"DEAL DAMAGE WITH THORN VOLLEY TO CHARGE"), Custom String("HEALING BLOSSOM ENERGY"), Left, 10, Color(Yellow), Color(White),
			Custom Color(250, 242, 195, 255), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);

	}

	{

		Lifeweaver;

	}

		Event Player.primary_charge -= 10;
	}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) JUNO - SPAWN ABILITY HUD")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Juno;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Has Spawned(Event Player) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, secondary_charge);
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, timer);
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, primary_charge);
		Event Player.primary_charge = 0;
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0]);
		Destroy Progress Bar HUD Text(Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0]);
		Destroy Progress Bar HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud[1]);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create Progress Bar HUD Text(Event Player, Event Player.secondary_charge, Custom String("HEALING POWER"), Left, 10, Color(Yellow),
			Color(White), Visible To Values and Color, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.charge_hud[1] = Last Text ID;
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = False;
		Event Player.Ability_Bool = False;
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_1);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_2);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_3);
		Event Player.secondary_charge = 8;
		Event Player.timer = 0;
		Event Player.heal_rate = 1.500;
		Start Healing Modification(All Players(Team 2), Event Player, Event Player.secondary_charge * 10,
			Receivers Healers and Healing Percent);
		Event Player.heal_power = Last Healing Modification ID;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) JUNO - HEAL CHARGE+")
{
	event
	{
		Player Dealt Damage;
		Team 2;
		Juno;
	}

	actions
	{
		Event Player.timer = 100;
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, secondary_charge);
		Skip If(Event Player.secondary_charge >= 100, 4);
		Skip If(Event Player.secondary_charge >= 50, 1);
		Event Player.secondary_charge += Event Damage * 0.660;
		Skip If(Event Player.secondary_charge < 50, 2);
		Event Player.secondary_charge += Event Damage * 0.330;
		Event Player.heal_rate = 2.500;
		Skip If(Event Player.secondary_charge <= 100, 1);
		Event Player.secondary_charge = 100;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) BAP - HEAL CHARGE HUD ON")

	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Baptiste;
	}

	{
		Event Player.secondary_charge > 0;
	}

	actions
	{
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud);
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud[0]);
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud[2]);
		Destroy Progress Bar HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud[1]);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 1);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Null, Null, Custom String(" \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n{0}",
			Round To Integer(Event Player.secondary_charge, Up)), Top, 8, Color(White), Color(Yellow), Color(Yellow),
			Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players == False, 1);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Null, Null, Custom String(" \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n{0}", Round To Integer(
			Event Player.secondary_charge, Up)), Top, 8, Color(White), Color(Yellow), Color(Yellow), Visible To and String,
			Default Visibility);
		Event Player.charge_hud[0] = Last Text ID;
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Null, Custom String(" \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\nHEAL CHARGE LOCK:"), Null, Top, 8.100, Color(
			White), Color(White), Color(White), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.charge_hud[2] = Last Text ID;
		Create Progress Bar HUD Text(Event Player, Event Player.timer, Null, Top, 8.200, Color(Orange), Color(White),
			Visible To Values and Color, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.charge_hud[1] = Last Text ID;

rule("CORE: (TEAM) PHARAH - TAG BOSS")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Pharah;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player.Aim[0] == True;
		(Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Interact)) && Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Jump))) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Destroy Icon(Global.BossTag);
		Event Player.Aim[0] = False;
		Event Player.timer = 10;
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.charge_hud[1]);
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud[0]);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Sombra Logo Sound, Color(White), All Players(All Teams), 100);
		Wait(0.100, Ignore Condition);
		Create Icon(All Players(Team 2), All Players(Team 1), Eye, Visible To and Position, Color(Team 1), True);
		Global.BossTag = Last Created Entity;
		Start Forcing Player Outlines(All Players(Team 1), All Players(Team 2), True, Color(Turquoise), Always);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 3);
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_StatusArray[1]);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(All Teams), Hero Icon String(Hero(Pharah)), Null, Custom String("Boss Tagged"), Right, -1.500, Color(
			Turquoise), Color(White), Color(Turquoise), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Global.BOSS_StatusArray[1] = Last Text ID;
		Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, timer, 0, 1, Destination and Rate);
		Wait Until(Event Player.timer <= 0.050 || Is Dead(Event Player), 10.100);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Sombra Logo Sound, Color(White), All Players(All Teams), 100);
		Stop Forcing Player Outlines(All Players(Team 1), All Players(Team 2));
		Destroy Icon(Global.BossTag);
		Event Player.timer = 20;
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_StatusArray[1]);
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud[0]);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 1);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Null, Null, Custom String(
			"   \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n {0}                              ", Round To Integer(
			Event Player.timer, Up)), Top, 8, Color(White), Color(White), Color(Turquoise), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players == False, 1);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Null, Null, Custom String(
			"   \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n {0}                              ", Round To Integer(Event Player.timer, Up)),
			Top, 8, Color(White), Color(White), Color(Turquoise), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.charge_hud[0] = Last Text ID;
		Wait Until(Event Player.timer == 0, 20.250);
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud[0]);
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, timer);
		Event Player.timer = 0;
		Skip If(!Is In Line of Sight(Eye Position(Event Player), All Players(Team 1), Barriers Do Not Block LOS)
			 || !Is In View Angle(Event Player, All Players(Team 1), Event Player.Aim[1]), 11);
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud[0]);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 1);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Null, Custom String(
			"   \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n {0} + {1}                                                                                     ",
			Input Binding String(Button(Interact)), Input Binding String(Button(Jump))), Custom String(
			" TAG BOSS                                                              "), Top, 8, Color(White), Color(White), Color(
			Turquoise), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Skip If(!Is Waiting For Players, 1);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Null, Custom String(
			"   \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n {0} + {1}                                                                                        ",
			Input Binding String(Button(Interact)), Input Binding String(Button(Jump))), Custom String(
			" TAG BOSS                                                              "), Top, 8, Color(White), Color(White), Color(
			Turquoise), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.charge_hud[0] = Last Text ID;
		Wait(0.025, Ignore Condition);
		Event Player.Aim[0] = True;
		Wait Until(!Is In View Angle(Event Player, All Players(Team 1), Event Player.Aim[1]) || !Is In Line of Sight(Eye Position(
			Event Player), All Players(Team 1), Barriers Do Not Block LOS), 99999);
		Event Player.Aim[0] = False;
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud[0]);
	}
}

		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Brigitte;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle == True;
		Is Alive(Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2)) == True;
		"OPEN ROLES switch off"
		(Is Waiting For Players || Global.A[0]) == True;
		Is In View Angle(Event Player, Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), Event Player.Aim[1]) == True;
		Is In Line of Sight(Eye Position(Event Player), Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), Barriers Do Not Block LOS) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud);
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud[0]);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 1);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Null, Custom String(
			"   \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n PRESS {0}                                                                                     ",
			Input Binding String(Button(Reload))), Custom String(
			" MERCY ARMOUR                                                              "), Top, 8, Color(White), Color(White), Color(
			Yellow), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players == False, 1);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Null, Custom String(
			"   \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n PRESS {0}                                                                                        ",
			Input Binding String(Button(Reload))), Custom String(
			" MERCY ARMOUR                                                              "), Top, 8, Color(White), Color(White), Color(
			Yellow), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.charge_hud[0] = Last Text ID;
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.charge_hud[1]);
		Create Effect(Event Player, Good Aura, Color(Orange), Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), 1, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.charge_hud[1] = Last Created Entity;
		Event Player.Aim[0] = True;
		Wait Until(!Is In View Angle(Event Player, Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), Event Player.Aim[1])
			 || !Is In Line of Sight(Eye Position(Event Player), Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), Barriers Do Not Block LOS)
			 || Is Dead(Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2)), 99999);
		Skip If(!Is In View Angle(Event Player, Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), Event Player.Aim[1]), 1);
		Wait(1, Restart When True);
		Event Player.Aim[0] = False;
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud[0]);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.charge_hud[1]);
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) REAP - LOSE ENERGY")

	event

		Player Died;
		Team 2;

	{
		Event Player.primary_charge < 100;
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Event Player.primary_charge > 25, 1);
		Event Player.primary_charge = 0;
		Skip If(Event Player.primary_charge <= 25, 1);
		Event Player.primary_charge -= 25;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (BOSS) ALL - BERSERK 1")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Is Waiting For Players == False;
		Has Spawned(Event Player) == True;
		Match Time >= 106;
		Player Stat(Event Player, All Damage Dealt) <= 0;
		Global.BERSERK[1] == -1;
		(Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Interact)) || Is Button Held(Host Player, Button(Interact))) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Wait Until((Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Interact)) || Is Button Held(Host Player, Button(Interact))) == False, 1.500);
		Skip If((Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Interact)) || Is Button Held(Host Player, Button(Interact))) == False, 3);
		Skip If(Global.BERSERK[1] == 0, 2);
		Global.BERSERK[0] = 1;
		Call Subroutine(BERSERK_activated);
	}
}

		Skip If(Global.BERSERK[1] == 0, 2);

	}
}

rule("SUB: ANTI-ENVIRO OOM")
{
	event
	{
		Subroutine;
		anti_enviro_OOM;
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Current Map != Map(Eichenwalde), 2);
		Skip If(X Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)) > 0.434 * Z Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)) + 63.503, 2);
		Teleport(Event Player, Vector(43.100, 5.300, -47.040));
		Skip(1);
		Teleport(Event Player, Nearest Walkable Position(Event Player));
		Skip If(Current Map != Map(Hanamura), 2);
		Skip If(Z Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)) > -1 * X Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)) - 119.030, 2);
		Teleport(Event Player, Vector(-36.180, 1.100, -82.850));
		Skip(1);
		Teleport(Event Player, Nearest Walkable Position(Event Player));
	}
}

rule("SUB: BERSERK ACTIVATED")
{
	event
	{
		Subroutine;
		BERSERK_activated;
	}

	actions
	{
		Global.BERSERK[2] = 1;
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Global.BERSERK[1] = 0;
		Set Match Time(Match Time / 2 + 0.500);
		Play Effect(All Players(Team 1), Good Explosion, Color(Red), Eye Position(Event Player) + Facing Direction Of(Event Player) * 1,
			5);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring Explosion Sound, Color(White), All Players(All Teams), 250);
		Skip If(Global.BERSERK[0] == 2, 5);
		Small Message(All Players(Team 1), Custom String("BERSERK ACTIVE"));
		Small Message(All Players(Team 2), Custom String("BOSS IS BERSERKING"));
		Global.MAX_TIME = 61;
		Global.BERSERK[1] = -2;
		Set Objective Description(All Players(All Teams), Custom String("BERSERK MATCH"), Visible To and String);
		Skip If(Global.BERSERK[0] == 1, 5);
		Small Message(All Players(Team 1), Custom String("DOUBLE BERSERK"));
		Small Message(All Players(Team 2), Custom String("BOSS IS DOUBLE BERSERKING"));
		Global.MAX_TIME = 31;
		Global.BERSERK[1] = 0;
		Set Objective Description(All Players(All Teams), Custom String("DOUBLE BERSERK MATCH"), Visible To and String);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Global.BERSERK[2] = 0;
	}
}

	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		All;
		Echo;
	}

	{

	}

	{

		Remove Health Pool From Player(Event Player.health_pool);
		Remove Health Pool From Player(Event Player.shield_pool);
		Remove Health Pool From Player(Event Player.armour_pool);
		Add Health Pool To Player(Event Player, Health, 175.500, True, False);
		Event Player.health_pool = Last Created Health Pool;
		Event Player.base_health = Max Health(Event Player);
		Event Player.base_shields = Max Health Of Type(Event Player, Shields);
		Skip(1);
		Set Max Health(Event Player, 99.875);
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) ANA - EQ HEAL")
{
	event
	{
		Player Dealt Healing;
		Team 2;
		Ana;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Ability != Button(Ability 2);
		Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 2)) > 10;
		Event Player.secondary_charge != 2;
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Event Player.secondary_charge == 0, 6);
		Set Ultimate Charge(Event Player, Ultimate Charge Percent(Event Player) + 1);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Event Player.secondary_charge = 2;
		Wait(0.750, Ignore Condition);
		Event Player.secondary_charge = 0;
		Skip(3);
		Event Player.secondary_charge = 2;
		Wait(0.750, Ignore Condition);

rule("CORE: (TEAM) SYM - USE STUN")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Symmetra;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player.Stunned != True;
		Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Ultimate)) == True;
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle == True;
		Event Player.primary_charge == 0;
	}

	actions
	{
		Press Button(Event Player, Button(Melee));
		Wait(0.350, Ignore Condition);
		Skip If(Is Meleeing(Event Player) == False, 33);
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = False;
		Event Player.Ability_Bool = True;
		Skip If(!Is True For Any(Players Within Radius(Eye Position(Event Player) + Facing Direction Of(Event Player) * 6, 8, All Teams,
			Surfaces), Current Array Element == Event Player), 16);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Bad Explosion, Color(White), Eye Position(Event Player) + Facing Direction Of(Event Player)
			* 6, 2);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Set Ultimate Charge(Event Player, Ultimate Charge Percent(Event Player) - 12);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Cassidy Flashbang Explosion Sound, Color(White), Eye Position(Event Player)
			+ Facing Direction Of(Event Player) * 6, 100);
		Set Status(Players Within Radius(Eye Position(Event Player) + Facing Direction Of(Event Player) * 6, 4.200, Team 1, Surfaces),
			Event Player, Stunned, 0.800);
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0]);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, primary_charge);
		Event Player.primary_charge = 12;
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Event Player.Ability_Bool = False;
		Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, primary_charge, 0, 1, Destination and Rate);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Round To Integer(Event Player.primary_charge, Up), Custom String("COOLDOWN"), Custom String(
			"PHOTONIC FLASH"), Left, 10, Color(Orange), Color(Orange), Color(Aqua), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0] = Last Text ID;
		Skip(14);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Bad Explosion, Color(White), Eye Position(Event Player) + Facing Direction Of(Event Player)
			* 1, 2);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Set Ultimate Charge(Event Player, Ultimate Charge Percent(Event Player) - 12);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Cassidy Flashbang Explosion Sound, Color(White), Eye Position(Event Player)
			+ Facing Direction Of(Event Player) * 1, 100);
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0]);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, primary_charge);
		Event Player.primary_charge = 12;
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Event Player.Ability_Bool = False;
		Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, primary_charge, 0, 1, Destination and Rate);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Round To Integer(Event Player.primary_charge, Up), Custom String("COOLDOWN"), Custom String(
			"PHOTONIC FLASH"), Left, 10, Color(Orange), Color(Orange), Color(Aqua), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0] = Last Text ID;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) LUCIO - MEGA AMP USE")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Lúcio;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle == True;
		Event Player.Stunned != True;
		Is Using Ability 2(Event Player) == True;
		Is In Alternate Form(Event Player) == False;
	}

	actions
	{
		Destroy In-World Text(Event Player.PlayerFX_1);
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0]);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Custom String("{0} {1}", Icon String(Arrow: Up), Ability Icon String(Hero(Lúcio), Button(
			Ability 2))), Custom String("-> playing"), Custom String("mega amp heal song {0} {1} {2}", Icon String(Arrow: Up),
			Ability Icon String(Hero(Lúcio), Button(Ability 2)), Ability Icon String(Hero(Baptiste), Button(Ability 1))), Left, 10, Color(
			Orange), Color(Green), Color(Yellow), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0] = Last Text ID;
		Event Player.Ability_Bool = True;
		Event Player.primary_charge = 0;
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Buff Explosion Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 25);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_1);
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_2);
		Wait(0.050, Ignore Condition);
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 2);
		Create Effect(Event Player, Good Aura, Color(Yellow), Event Player + Vector(0, Event Player.Z[4], 0) + Facing Direction Of(
			Event Player), 1.666, Visible To Position and Radius);
		Event Player.PlayerFX_2 = Last Created Entity;
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Play Effect(Remove From Array(All Players(All Teams), Event Player), Good Pickup Effect, Color(Yellow), Event Player, 1);
		Heal(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 11.700, Team 2, Surfaces And Enemy Barriers), Event Player, 5);
		Heal(Remove From Array(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 11.700, Team 2, Surfaces And Enemy Barriers), Players On Hero(Hero(
			Mercy), Team 2)), Event Player, 57.500);
		Heal(Filtered Array(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 11.700, Team 2, Surfaces And Enemy Barriers),
			Current Array Element.Z[3] == 1), Event Player, 62.500);
		Wait(0.737, Abort When False);
		Play Effect(Remove From Array(All Players(All Teams), Event Player), Good Pickup Effect, Color(Yellow), Event Player, 1);
		Heal(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 11.700, Team 2, Surfaces And Enemy Barriers), Event Player, 5);
		Heal(Remove From Array(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 11.700, Team 2, Surfaces And Enemy Barriers), Players On Hero(Hero(
			Mercy), Team 2)), Event Player, 57.500);
		Heal(Filtered Array(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 11.700, Team 2, Surfaces And Enemy Barriers),
			Current Array Element.Z[3] == 1), Event Player, 62.500);
		Wait(0.737, Abort When False);
		Play Effect(Remove From Array(All Players(All Teams), Event Player), Good Pickup Effect, Color(Yellow), Event Player, 1);
		Heal(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 11.700, Team 2, Surfaces And Enemy Barriers), Event Player, 5);
		Heal(Remove From Array(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 11.700, Team 2, Surfaces And Enemy Barriers), Players On Hero(Hero(
			Mercy), Team 2)), Event Player, 57.500);
		Heal(Filtered Array(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 11.700, Team 2, Surfaces And Enemy Barriers),
			Current Array Element.Z[3] == 1), Event Player, 62.500);
		Wait(0.737, Abort When False);
		Play Effect(Remove From Array(All Players(All Teams), Event Player), Good Pickup Effect, Color(Yellow), Event Player, 1);
		Heal(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 11.700, Team 2, Surfaces And Enemy Barriers), Event Player, 5);
		Heal(Remove From Array(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 11.700, Team 2, Surfaces And Enemy Barriers), Players On Hero(Hero(
			Mercy), Team 2)), Event Player, 57.500);
		Heal(Filtered Array(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 11.700, Team 2, Surfaces And Enemy Barriers),
			Current Array Element.Z[3] == 1), Event Player, 62.500);
		Wait(0.700, Abort When False);
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = False;
	}
}

{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Lúcio;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle == False;
		Event Player.Ability_Bool == False;
		Is In Alternate Form(Event Player) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Wait(1.600, Abort When False);
		Event Player.primary_charge += Count Of(Remove From Array(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 12, Team 2,
			Surfaces And Enemy Barriers), Event Player)) * 0.750;
		Skip If(!Is Using Ability 2(Event Player), 1);
		Event Player.primary_charge += Count Of(Remove From Array(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 12, Team 2,
			Surfaces And Enemy Barriers), Event Player)) * 2.250;
		Wait(0.016, Abort When False);
		Loop If Condition Is True;
	}
}

		(Is Using Ability 2(Event Player) && Event Ability == Button(Ability 2)) == True;
		Ultimate Charge Percent(Event Player) < 100;
	}

	actions
	{
		Set Ultimate Charge(Event Player, Ultimate Charge Percent(Event Player) + 3.300);
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) ALL - HARD COOLDOWNS")
{
	event
	{
		Player Died;
		Team 2;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Is Waiting For Players == False;
		Array Contains(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Hero(Mei), Hero(Sigma), Hero(Brigitte), Hero(Orisa), Hero(Genji), Hero(Ana), Hero(Baptiste),
			Hero(Lúcio), Hero(Kiriko), Hero(Lifeweaver), Hero(Sombra), Hero(Mauga)), Hero Of(Event Player)) == True;
		Is Dead(Event Player) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Ana) && Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Reinhardt) && Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Sombra),
			6);
		Abort If(Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 1)) <= 9);
		Event Player.CD_saver = Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 1));
		Wait Until(Is Alive(Event Player), 9);
		Skip If(Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Ana) && Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Reinhardt) && Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Sombra),
			2);
		Skip If(Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 1)) > Event Player.CD_saver - 9, 1);
		Set Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 1), Event Player.CD_saver - 7);
		Skip If(Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Orisa) && Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Mei) && Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Baptiste)
			&& Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Sigma) && Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Kiriko) && Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Lifeweaver)
			&& Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Mauga) && Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Genji), 7);
		Wait(5.100, Abort When False);
		Abort If(Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 2)) <= 3.900);
		Event Player.CD_saver = Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 2));
		Wait Until(Is Alive(Event Player), 9);
		Skip If(Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Orisa) && Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Mei) && Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Baptiste)
			&& Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Sigma) && Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Kiriko) && Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Lifeweaver)
			&& Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Mauga) && Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Genji), 2);
		Skip If(Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 2)) > Event Player.CD_saver - 3.900, 1);
		Set Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 2), Event Player.CD_saver - 1.900);
		Skip If(Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Lúcio), 7);
		Wait(5, Abort When False);
		Abort If(Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Secondary Fire)) <= 4);
		Event Player.CD_saver = Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Secondary Fire));
		Wait Until(Is Alive(Event Player), 9);
		Skip If(Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Lúcio), 2);
		Skip If(Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Secondary Fire)) > Event Player.CD_saver - 4, 1);
		Set Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Secondary Fire), Event Player.CD_saver - 2);
		Skip If(Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Brigitte), 7);
		Wait(5, Abort When False);
		Abort If(Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Primary Fire)) <= 4);
		Event Player.CD_saver = Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Primary Fire));
		Wait Until(Is Alive(Event Player), 9);
		Skip If(Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Brigitte), 2);
		Skip If(Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Primary Fire)) > Event Player.CD_saver - 4, 1);
		Set Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Primary Fire), Event Player.CD_saver - 2);
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) JQ knife stun")
{
	event
	{
		Player Dealt Damage;
		Team 2;
		Junker Queen;
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Is Meleeing(Event Player), 20);
		Skip If(Is Dead(Event Player), 19);
		Skip If(Event Ability != Button(Secondary Fire), 18);
		Skip If(Event Player.primary_charge == Custom String("G.STUN"), 17);
		Set Status(Victim, Event Player, Stunned, 0.900);
		Event Player.primary_charge = Custom String("G.STUN");
		Event Player.secondary_charge = 12;
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0]);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Custom String("- {0} -", Round To Integer(Event Player.secondary_charge, Up)), Custom String(
			"Stun Cooldown"), Custom String("Jagged Blade Stun"), Left, 10, Color(Orange), Color(Orange), Color(Red),
			Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0] = Last Text ID;
		Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, secondary_charge, 0, 1, Destination and Rate);
		Wait Until(Is Dead(Event Player), 12);
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, secondary_charge);
		Event Player.secondary_charge = 0;
		Skip If(Hero Of(Event Player) != Hero(Junker Queen), 5);
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0]);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Custom String("{0} {1}", Ability Icon String(Hero(Junker Queen), Button(Secondary Fire)),
			Icon String(Dizzy)), Custom String("Damage with knife to stun Boss"), Custom String("Jagged Blade Stun"), Left, 10, Color(Red),
			Color(White), Color(Red), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0] = Last Text ID;
		Event Player.primary_charge = Custom String("G.READY");
	}
}

rule("CORE: (BOSS) RAM JUMP")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		Ramattra;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player.Ability_Bool == True;
		(!Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Ability 1)) || Event Player.secondary_charge >= 5) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_2);
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = False;
		Clear Status(Event Player, Rooted);
		Set Move Speed(Event Player, 150);
		Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, primary_charge);
		Event Player.secondary_charge = 13;
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BOSS_AbilityKey);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(Team 1), Round To Integer(Event Player.secondary_charge, Up), Custom String("Cooldown"), Custom String(
			"NEMESIS JUMP"), Left, 1, Color(Orange), Color(White), Color(Rose), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Global.BOSS_AbilityKey = Last Text ID;
		Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, primary_charge, 5, 1, Destination and Rate);
		Skip If(Event Player.primary_charge < 2.500, 2);
		Apply Impulse(Event Player, Up, 5 * Event Player.primary_charge, To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
		Skip(1);
		Apply Impulse(Event Player, Up, 12.500, To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring Explosion, Color(Rose), Event Player, 4);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring Explosion Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 100);
		Wait(0.200, Ignore Condition);
		Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, secondary_charge, 0, 1, Destination and Rate);
		Wait Until(Is On Ground(Event Player) || Is Dead(Event Player), 999);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Doomfist Meteor Strike Impact Sound, Color(White), Position Of(Event Player) + Vector(0, 1, 0),
			500);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring Explosion, Color(White), Position Of(Event Player) + Vector(0, 0.200, 0), 25);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Bad Explosion, Color(Rose), Position Of(Event Player) + Vector(0, 1, 0), 8);
		Apply Impulse(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 13, Team 2, Surfaces And Enemy Barriers), Up, 6.666, To World,
			Cancel Contrary Motion);
		Set Status(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 13, Team 2, Surfaces And Enemy Barriers), Event Player, Rooted, 0.666);
		Damage(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 13, Team 2, Surfaces And Enemy Barriers), Event Player,
			4 * Event Player.primary_charge);
		Damage(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 8, Team 2, Surfaces And Enemy Barriers), Event Player, 6 * Event Player.primary_charge);
		Damage(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 4, Team 2, Surfaces And Enemy Barriers), Event Player, 6 * Event Player.primary_charge);
		Damage(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 1.200, Team 2, Surfaces And Enemy Barriers), Event Player,
			8 * Event Player.primary_charge);
		Set Move Speed(Event Player, 100);
		Event Player.Ability_Bool = False;
	}
}

rule("(BOSS) KIRIKO STEP AIM")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		Kiriko;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player.Ability_Bool == False;
		Event Player.primary_charge == 0;
		Is True For Any(Filtered Array(All Players(Team 2), Is Alive(Current Array Element)), (Is In View Angle(Event Player,
			Current Array Element, 3) && !Is In Line of Sight(Eye Position(Event Player), Current Array Element, Barriers Do Not Block LOS))
			== True) == True;
		Is In Line of Sight(Eye Position(Player Closest To Reticle(Event Player, Team 2)), Eye Position(Player Closest To Reticle(
			Event Player, Team 2)) + Facing Direction Of(Event Player) * 4, Barriers Do Not Block LOS) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_2);
		Create Effect(Event Player, Good Aura, Color(Aqua), Player Closest To Reticle(Event Player, Team 2), 1, Position and Radius);
		Event Player.PlayerFX_2 = Last Created Entity;
		Destroy In-World Text(Event Player.PlayerFX_0);
		Create In-World Text(Event Player, Custom String("{0} {1}", Input Binding String(Button(Ability 1)), Hero Icon String(Hero Of(
			Player Closest To Reticle(Event Player, Team 2)))), Player Closest To Reticle(Event Player, Team 2), 0.750, Do Not Clip,
			Visible To Position and String, Color(White), Default Visibility);
		Event Player.PlayerFX_0 = Last Text ID;
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = True;
		Wait Until(Is True For All(All Players(Team 2), (!Is In View Angle(Event Player, Current Array Element, 3)
			 || !Is In Line of Sight(Eye Position(Event Player), Current Array Element, Barriers Do Not Block LOS)
			 || Event Player.Ability_Bool || Is Dead(Event Player)
			 || Event Player.primary_charge == 1 || !Is In Line of Sight(Eye Position(Player Closest To Reticle(Event Player,
			Team 2)), Eye Position(Player Closest To Reticle(Event Player, Team 2)) + Facing Direction Of(Event Player) * 4,
			Barriers Do Not Block LOS)) == True), 999);
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = False;
		Destroy Effect(Event Player.PlayerFX_2);
		Destroy In-World Text(Event Player.PlayerFX_0);
	}
}

rule("(BOSS) KIRIKO STEP USE")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		Kiriko;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle == True;
		Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Ability 1)) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(!Is In Line of Sight(Eye Position(Player Closest To Reticle(Event Player, Team 2)), Eye Position(Player Closest To Reticle(
			Event Player, Team 2)) + Facing Direction Of(Event Player) * 4, Barriers Do Not Block LOS), 20);
		Event Player.Ability_Bool = True;
		Event Player.Ability_Toggle = False;
		Event Player.primary_charge = 1;
		Event Player.secondary_charge = Player Closest To Reticle(Event Player, Team 2);
		Disallow Button(Event Player, Button(Primary Fire));
		Disallow Button(Event Player, Button(Melee));
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Good Explosion, Color(Team 1), Event Player, 2);
		Wait(0.025, Ignore Condition);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Buff Impact Sound, Color(Team 1), Event Player, 50);
		Wait(0.025, Ignore Condition);
		Teleport(Event Player, Eye Position(Event Player.secondary_charge) + Facing Direction Of(Event Player) * 4);
		Start Facing(Event Player, Facing Direction Of(Event Player) * -1, 9999, To World, None);
		Wait(0.025, Ignore Condition);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Good Explosion, Color(Team 1), Event Player, 1);
		Wait(0.025, Ignore Condition);
		Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Buff Impact Sound, Color(Team 1), Event Player, 25);
		Stop Facing(Event Player);
		Allow Button(Event Player, Button(Primary Fire));
		Allow Button(Event Player, Button(Melee));
		Set Ability 1 Enabled(Event Player, False);
	}
}

rule("CORE: (ALL) TRACK CC")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		All;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		(Has Status(Event Player, Hacked) || Has Status(Event Player, Knocked Down) || Has Status(Event Player, Asleep) || Has Status(
			Event Player, Frozen) || Has Status(Event Player, Stunned) || Is Communicating Any Emote(Event Player) || Is Alive(
			Event Player) != True || !Has Spawned(Event Player)) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Event Player.Stunned = True;
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Wait Until(!Has Status(Event Player, Hacked) && !Has Status(Event Player, Knocked Down) && !Has Status(Event Player, Asleep)
			&& !Has Status(Event Player, Frozen) && !Has Status(Event Player, Stunned) && Is Alive(Event Player)
			&& !Is Communicating Any Emote(Event Player) && Has Spawned(Event Player), 99999);
		Event Player.Stunned = False;
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Loop If Condition Is True;
	}
}

		Wait(1, Ignore Condition);

		Set Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 2), Event Player.secondary_charge);
		Wait Until(Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 2)) == 0, 13.500);
		Event Player.primary_charge = 0;

rule("CORE: (TEAM) VENDETTA ULT LOOP")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Vendetta;
	}

	conditions
	{
		(Event Player.primary_charge != 6 && Ultimate Charge Percent(Event Player) == 100 && !Is Using Ultimate(Event Player))
			== True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Event Player.primary_charge > 0, 1);
		Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ultimate));
		Wait(0.250, Ignore Condition);
		Loop If Condition Is True;
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0]);
		Event Player.primary_charge = 6;
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.charge_hud);
		Set Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 2), 0);
		Set Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 1), 0);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Ability Icon String(Hero(Vendetta), Button(Ultimate)), Custom String(
			"base cooldowns reduce as ultimate charges"), Custom String("auto charge + activation"), Left, 10, Color(Red), Color(White),
			Color(Gray), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0] = Last Text ID;
		Abort If Condition Is False;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) ANRAN - IGNITION ACTIVE")
{
	event
	{
		Player Dealt Damage;
		Team 2;
		Anran;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Has Status(Victim, Burning) == True;
		(Event Ability == Button(Ability 1) || Event Ability == Button(Ability 2) || Event Ability == Button(Ultimate)
			|| Event Damage > 2 * Global.BossResistanceStat * (Global.BossDamageReceived / 100)) == True;
		Event Ability != Button(Melee);
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Event Player.timer != 0, 13);
		Event Player.Ability_Bool = True;
		Global.BossDamageReceived *= 1.160;
		Set Damage Received(Victim, Global.BossDamageReceived);
		Event Player.timer = 3;
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0]);
		Destroy Progress Bar HUD Text(Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0]);
		Create Progress Bar HUD Text(Event Player, 100 * (Event Player.timer / 3), Custom String("BOSS IGNITION"), Left, 10, Color(Orange),
			Color(Red), Visible To Values and Color, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0] = Last Text ID;
		Skip If(Is Waiting For Players, 4);
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BossStatus_Burning);
		Create HUD Text(All Players(All Teams), Icon String(Fire), Null, Custom String("Boss Ignited"), Right, -1.500, Color(Red), Color(
			Red), Color(Red), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Global.BossStatus_Burning = Last Text ID;
		Skip(2);
		Event Player.Ability_Bool = True;
		Event Player.timer = 3;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) ANRAN - IGNITION EXPIRE")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 2;
		Anran;
	}

	conditions
	{
		(Is Dead(Event Player) || Event Player.timer == 0 || !Has Status(All Players(Team 1), Burning)) == True;
		Event Player.Ability_Bool == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Event Player.Ability_Bool = False;
		Event Player.timer = 0;
		Call Subroutine(BossIgnitionExpire);
		Destroy HUD Text(Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0]);
		Destroy Progress Bar HUD Text(Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0]);
		Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
		Create HUD Text(Event Player, Icon String(Fire), Custom String("IGNITED BOSS TAKES MORE DAMAGE FROM ALLIES"), Custom String(
			"IGNITION EFFECT"), Left, 10, Color(Orange), Color(White), Color(Yellow), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
		Event Player.team_abilityHUD[0] = Last Text ID;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (TEAM) ANRAN - LEAVES MATCH, IGNITION EXPIRE")
{
	event
	{
		Player Left Match;
		Team 2;
		Anran;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Event Player.Ability_Bool == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Event Player.Ability_Bool = False;
		Call Subroutine(BossIgnitionExpire);
	}
}

rule("SUB: BOSS IGNITION EXPIRE")
{
	event
	{
		Subroutine;
		BossIgnitionExpire;
	}

	actions
	{
		Global.BossDamageReceived *= 10 / 11.6;
		Set Damage Received(All Players(Team 1), Global.BossDamageReceived);
		Destroy HUD Text(Global.BossStatus_Burning);
	}
}

rule("CORE: (BOSS) ALL / (TEAM) ANRAN - DAMAGE AMPLIFIED")
{
	event
	{
		Player Took Damage;
		Team 1;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Global.BossStatus_Burning != Null;
		Is Waiting For Players == False;
		Has Status(Event Player, Burning) == True;
		Is True For Any(Players On Hero(Hero(Anran), Team 2), Current Array Element.Ability_Bool == True) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Global.BossIgnitedDamageTaken += Event Damage / 7.25;
	}
}

rule("CORE: (BOSS) ALL - DAMAGE RECEIVED")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		Team 1;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Has Spawned(Event Player) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Global.BossDamageReceived = 100;
		Set Damage Received(Event Player, Global.BossDamageReceived);
	}
}

rule("temp bug fix - hazard ammo")
{
	event
	{
		Ongoing - Each Player;
		All;
		Hazard;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Has Spawned(Event Player) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Skip If(Team Of(Event Player) == Team 1, 2);
		Set Ammo(Event Player, 0, 6);
		Set Max Ammo(Event Player, 0, 6);
		Skip If(Team Of(Event Player) == Team 2, 2);
		Set Ammo(Event Player, 0, 3);
		Set Max Ammo(Event Player, 0, 3);
	}
}

rule("LastDamageNumber Add")
{
	event
	{
		Player Dealt Damage;
		Team 2;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Team Of(Victim) == Team 1;
	}

	actions
	{
		Event Player.LastDamageNumber += Event Damage;
		Wait(0.048, Restart When True);
		Event Player.LastDamageNumber = 0;
	}
}

rule("Damage Numbers 0")
{
	event
	{
		Player Dealt Damage;
		Team 2;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Team Of(Victim) == Team 1;
		(Event Player.LastDamageNumberInstance == 0 || Event Player.LastDamageNumberInstance == 2) == True;
	}

	actions
	{
		Destroy In-World Text(Event Player.LastDamage[0]);
		Wait(0.032, Ignore Condition);
		Destroy In-World Text(Event Player.LastDamage[0]);
		Skip If(Event Player.LastDamageNumber == 0, 18);
		Skip If(Event Player.LastDamageNumber >= 10, 2);
		Event Player.LastDamageNumberTime[0] = 0.333;
		Create In-World Text(All Players(Team 2), Event Player.LastDamageNumber, Eye Position(Victim) + Vector(Random Real(-0.500, 0.500),
			Random Real(0.500, 1), Random Real(-0.500, 0.500)), 1, Clip Against Surfaces, Visible To, Color(White), Default Visibility);
		Skip If((Event Player.LastDamageNumber < 10 || Event Player.LastDamageNumber >= 45), 2);
		Event Player.LastDamageNumberTime[0] = 0.500;
		Create In-World Text(All Players(Team 2), Event Player.LastDamageNumber, Eye Position(Victim) + Vector(Random Real(-0.500, 0.500),
			Random Real(0.500, 1), Random Real(-0.500, 0.500)), 1.500, Clip Against Surfaces, Visible To, Custom Color(255, 255, 200, 255),
			Default Visibility);
		Skip If((Event Player.LastDamageNumber < 45 || Event Player.LastDamageNumber >= 90), 2);
		Event Player.LastDamageNumberTime[0] = 0.666;
		Create In-World Text(All Players(Team 2), Event Player.LastDamageNumber, Eye Position(Victim) + Vector(Random Real(-0.500, 0.500),
			Random Real(0.500, 1), Random Real(-0.500, 0.500)), 2, Clip Against Surfaces, Visible To, Custom Color(255, 255, 100, 255),
			Default Visibility);
		Skip If((Event Player.LastDamageNumber < 90 || Event Player.LastDamageNumber >= 160), 2);
		Event Player.LastDamageNumberTime[0] = 1;
		Create In-World Text(All Players(Team 2), Event Player.LastDamageNumber, Eye Position(Victim) + Vector(Random Real(-0.500, 0.500),
			Random Real(0.500, 1), Random Real(-0.500, 0.500)), 2.500, Clip Against Surfaces, Visible To, Color(Yellow),
			Default Visibility);
		Skip If(Event Player.LastDamageNumber < 160, 2);
		Event Player.LastDamageNumberTime[0] = 1.250;
		Create In-World Text(All Players(Team 2), Event Player.LastDamageNumber, Eye Position(Victim) + Vector(Random Real(-0.500, 0.500),
			Random Real(0.500, 1), Random Real(-0.500, 0.500)), 3, Clip Against Surfaces, Visible To, Color(Orange), Default Visibility);
		Event Player.LastDamage[0] = Last Text ID;
		Event Player.LastDamageNumberInstance = 1;
		Wait(Event Player.LastDamageNumberTime[0], Restart When True);
		Destroy In-World Text(Event Player.LastDamage[0]);
	}
}

rule("Damage Numbers 1")
{
	event
	{
		Player Dealt Damage;
		Team 2;
		All;
	}

	conditions
	{
		Team Of(Victim) == Team 1;
		Event Player.LastDamageNumberInstance == 1;
	}

	actions
	{
		Destroy In-World Text(Event Player.LastDamage[0]);
		Wait(0.032, Ignore Condition);
		Destroy In-World Text(Event Player.LastDamage[1]);
		Skip If(Event Player.LastDamageNumber == 0, 18);
		Skip If(Event Player.LastDamageNumber >= 10, 2);
		Event Player.LastDamageNumberTime[1] = 0.333;
		Create In-World Text(All Players(Team 2), Event Player.LastDamageNumber, Eye Position(Victim) + Vector(Random Real(-0.500, 0.500),
			Random Real(0.500, 1), Random Real(-0.500, 0.500)), 1, Clip Against Surfaces, Visible To, Color(White), Default Visibility);
		Skip If((Event Player.LastDamageNumber < 10 || Event Player.LastDamageNumber >= 45), 2);
		Event Player.LastDamageNumberTime[1] = 0.500;
		Create In-World Text(All Players(Team 2), Event Player.LastDamageNumber, Eye Position(Victim) + Vector(Random Real(-0.500, 0.500),
			Random Real(0.500, 1), Random Real(-0.500, 0.500)), 1.500, Clip Against Surfaces, Visible To, Custom Color(255, 255, 200, 255),
			Default Visibility);
		Skip If((Event Player.LastDamageNumber < 45 || Event Player.LastDamageNumber >= 90), 2);
		Event Player.LastDamageNumberTime[1] = 0.666;
		Create In-World Text(All Players(Team 2), Event Player.LastDamageNumber, Eye Position(Victim) + Vector(Random Real(-0.500, 0.500),
			Random Real(0.500, 1), Random Real(-0.500, 0.500)), 2, Clip Against Surfaces, Visible To, Custom Color(255, 255, 100, 255),
			Default Visibility);
		Skip If((Event Player.LastDamageNumber < 90 || Event Player.LastDamageNumber >= 160), 2);
		Event Player.LastDamageNumberTime[1] = 1;
		Create In-World Text(All Players(Team 2), Event Player.LastDamageNumber, Eye Position(Victim) + Vector(Random Real(-0.500, 0.500),
			Random Real(0.500, 1), Random Real(-0.500, 0.500)), 2.500, Clip Against Surfaces, Visible To, Color(Yellow),
			Default Visibility);
		Skip If(Event Player.LastDamageNumber < 160, 2);
		Event Player.LastDamageNumberTime[1] = 1.250;
		Create In-World Text(All Players(Team 2), Event Player.LastDamageNumber, Eye Position(Victim) + Vector(Random Real(-0.500, 0.500),
			Random Real(0.500, 1), Random Real(-0.500, 0.500)), 3, Clip Against Surfaces, Visible To, Color(Orange), Default Visibility);
		Event Player.LastDamage[1] = Last Text ID;
		Event Player.LastDamageNumberInstance = 2;
		Wait(Event Player.LastDamageNumberTime[1], Restart When True);
		Destroy In-World Text(Event Player.LastDamage[1]);
	}
